  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_1fde1c7c-d849-4ca7-85ff-1d9d9e001733'
      });
    }
    
    var initializeSiwa = function() {
      var APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL =  "https://appleid.cdn-apple.com/appleauth/static/jsapi/appleid/1/en_US/appleid.auth.js"
      loadScript(APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL, initAppleId);
    };

      initAppleId();

      initializeSiwa();

      <div id="description" class="readable stacked" style="right:0">
        
<span id="freeTextContainer9245697983661185278"><i>To take back life, one must first face death...</i><br/><br/><b>One man stripped of his freedom, his morals...his life.</b><br/><br/>Conditioned in captivity to maim, to kill and to slaughter, prisoner 818 becomes an unremorseful, unrivaled and unstoppable fighter in the ring. Violence is all he knows. Death and brutality are the masters of his fate.<br/><br/>After years of incarceration in an underground hell, o</span>
  <span id="freeText9245697983661185278" style="display:none"><i>To take back life, one must first face death...</i><br /><br /><b>One man stripped of his freedom, his morals...his life.</b><br /><br />Conditioned in captivity to maim, to kill and to slaughter, prisoner 818 becomes an unremorseful, unrivaled and unstoppable fighter in the ring. Violence is all he knows. Death and brutality are the masters of his fate.<br /><br />After years of incarceration in an underground hell, only one thought occupies his mind: revenge...bloody, slow and violent revenge.<br /><br />Revenge on the man who lied.<br /><br />Revenge on the man who wronged him.<br /><br />Revenge on the man who condemned him and turned him into this: a rage-fueled killing machine. A monster void of humanity; a monster filled with hate.<br /><br />And no one will stand in the way of getting what he wants.<br /><br /><b>One woman stripped of her freedom, her morals...her life.</b><br /><br />Kisa Volkova is the only daughter of Kirill ‘The Silencer’ Volkov, head of the infamous ‘Triad’ bosses of New York's Russian Bratva. Her life is protected. In reality, it’s a virtual prison. Her father’s savage treatment of his rivals and his lucrative and coveted underground gambling ring—The Dungeon—ensures too many enemies lurk at their door. <br /><br />She dreams to be set free.<br /><br />Kisa has known only cruelty and loss in her short life. As manager of her father’s death match enterprise, only grief and pain fill her days. Her mafia boss father, in her world, rules absolute. And her fiancé, Alik Durov, is no better; the Dungeon’s five-time champion, a stone-cold killer, the treasured son of her father’s best friend, and her very own—and much resented—personal guard. Unrivaled in both strength and social standing, Alik controls every facet of Kisa’s life, dominates her every move; keeps her subdued and dead inside...then one night changes everything. <br /><br />While working for her church—the only reprieve in her constant surveillance—Kisa stumbles across a tattooed, scarred, but stunningly beautiful homeless man on the streets. Something about him stirs feelings deep within her; familiar yet impossibly forbidden desires. He doesn’t talk. Doesn’t communicate with anyone. He’s a man beyond saving, and a man she must quickly forget...for both their sakes. <br /><br />But when weeks later, out of the blue and to her complete surprise, he’s announced as the replacement fighter in The Dungeon, Kisa knows she’s in a whole lot of trouble. He’s built, ripped and lethally unforgiving to his opponents, leaving fear in his wake and the look of death in his eyes. <br /><br />Kisa becomes obsessed with him. Yearns for him. Craves his touch. Needs to possess this mysterious man...this man they call Raze.<br /><br /><i>Dark Contemporary Romance. Contains explicit sexual situations, excessive violence, disturbingly sensitive and taboo subjects, offensive language and mature topics. Recommended for age 18 years and up.</i></span>
  <a data-text-id="9245697983661185278" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

      </div>

  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1107123691" />
    <a title="Tillie Cole" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/17628953-tillie-cole"><img alt="Tillie Cole" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1517004375p2/17628953.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1107123691?book_show_action=true">Nov 15, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Tillie Cole" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Tillie Cole" href="/user/show/17628953-tillie-cole">Tillie Cole</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span> (Review from the author)


        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1107123691" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13086703884580276095">RAZE is a VERY different book for me to have written. But I have to admit that it consumed me, made my heart pound with what might happen, how the story would develop, and the characters were so real in my mind that the novel took me very little time to write. I just let the characters live in my head, and take me where they wanted the story to go. RAZE has now found a special place in my heart. I LOVE this man so deeply that he makes my soul ache!<br/>RAZE, the man, the fighter, the monster, is dark</span>
  <span id="freeText13086703884580276095" style="display:none">RAZE is a VERY different book for me to have written. But I have to admit that it consumed me, made my heart pound with what might happen, how the story would develop, and the characters were so real in my mind that the novel took me very little time to write. I just let the characters live in my head, and take me where they wanted the story to go. RAZE has now found a special place in my heart. I LOVE this man so deeply that he makes my soul ache!<br />RAZE, the man, the fighter, the monster, is dark, tortured, and so insanely extreme in every conceivable way that sometimes I forgot how to breathe when bringing him to life on the page.<br /><br />If you like fast-paced, heart-thumping, star-crossed lover based novels, then dive into RAZE!!!<br /><br />Hope you all enjoy it!!!!<br /><br /><br />If you are a blogger and you would like to part of the RAZE Book Blog Tour, please follow the link below:<br /><br />RAZE<br /><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://docs.google.com/forms/d/1vSPr2A78FVt40cMKfXH1bf7Qz04YbjPQiEkrRvjLpRM/viewform">https://docs.google.com/forms/d/1vSPr...</a></span>
  <a data-text-id="13086703884580276095" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_1105322102" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1105322102" />
    <a title="Christy" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/11284813-christy"><img alt="Christy" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1594293998p2/11284813.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1105322102?book_show_action=true">Nov 13, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Christy" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Christy" href="/user/show/11284813-christy">Christy</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1105322102" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16247669084376646649"><b>5+ “Can I have you” stars!</b><br/><br/><a href='http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%206/67a14401-c4ad-4eca-87c9-ac45673f085c_zpsbd3eb216.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1420020397i/13154833.jpg' alt=' photo 67a14401-c4ad-4eca-87c9-ac45673f085c_zpsbd3eb216.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><i>
  <blockquote>Their love story began on the day she was born.</blockquote>
</i><br/>Tillie Cole has been <b>that</b> author for me this year. Every year it seems, there is one author that comes out of nowhere and I am just completely taken by their books. I have read 6 Tillie Cole books this year, and 3 of them have made it on my top favorite lists. Her writing is addictive, her stories are so different from one another, yet all unbelievably good. This book was her most raw and gritty book yet. It was dow</span>
  <span id="freeText16247669084376646649" style="display:none"><b>5+ “Can I have you” stars!</b><br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%206/67a14401-c4ad-4eca-87c9-ac45673f085c_zpsbd3eb216.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1420020397i/13154833.jpg" alt=" photo 67a14401-c4ad-4eca-87c9-ac45673f085c_zpsbd3eb216.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><i>
  <blockquote>Their love story began on the day she was born.</blockquote>
</i><br>Tillie Cole has been <b>that</b> author for me this year. Every year it seems, there is one author that comes out of nowhere and I am just completely taken by their books. I have read 6 Tillie Cole books this year, and 3 of them have made it on my top favorite lists. Her writing is addictive, her stories are so different from one another, yet all unbelievably good. This book was her most raw and gritty book yet. It was down right gruesome at times. It’s one of those books that is going to be difficult for a lot of people to read because of the content. But under all that, it has to be one of the most beautiful love stories I have read and it’s definitely a favorite of 2014. <br><br>Number 818, or Raze has escaped the place he’s been ever since he was a boy. A place where he was tortured and brainwashed. A place where he was trained to be a fighter. Not a normal fighter, no, a kill or be killed kind of fighter. When you’re fighting to the death, you fight to kill.<br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%206/a8bb3f91-6f04-4c4f-a80f-a3eed1e2aadc_zps6edd6560.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1420020397i/13154834.jpg" alt=" photo a8bb3f91-6f04-4c4f-a80f-a3eed1e2aadc_zps6edd6560.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Now that he’s out, he only has one memory from his past to go on to seek what he wants most. Revenge. Raze doesn’t know who he is, if he has family, anything like that. He knows he is a killer and he’s going to do what he does best. Find the man that put him where he was, and kill him. He’s found Alix and is preparing, but there is this girl. A girl with familiar eyes. The first person he can ever remember feeling the need to be near, the need to protect. <br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%206/25996215-6e95-458e-a570-0e2e3be2dee5_zpsd08b38ec.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1420020397i/13154835.jpg" alt=" photo 25996215-6e95-458e-a570-0e2e3be2dee5_zpsd08b38ec.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Kisa Volkova is a Russian Mafia princess. She lives a sheltered and protected life. Then she meets Raze. This man is dangerous, she can tell. But there is something about him that draws him to her. She can’t stay away and she doesn’t want to. No matter how much she should. No matter how destructive it could be for them to be near each other, she has to be near him. <br><br>Raze and Kisa can’t fight this instant connection and attraction they have to one another. Being together is dangerous for them both, especially Kisa, but she can’t stay away from him. <br><i>
  <blockquote>I had never felt this before. Never felt this overwhelming lust, this consuming level of instant attraction... this raw and insatiable need to be with a man. It was dangerous. It was haunting. It was forbidden. And although it was wrong, it felt so perfectly right.</blockquote>
</i><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%206/b11a8513-3091-4fbc-a3d6-68b3dbc5c1b3_zps3dc87f3a.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1420020397i/13154836.jpg" alt=" photo b11a8513-3091-4fbc-a3d6-68b3dbc5c1b3_zps3dc87f3a.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>There is so much more I want to say about this story, about what happens, about the stunning revelations and about the intense moments. And if you read the book we can talk all day about it, but I’m not writing any of it here. It’s one of those stories you have to read for yourself. The things in this book are so exceptionally beautiful at times it brought me to tears. How things came together. Just wow. <br><br>Raze was such a beautiful and strong man. Reading about what he went through will destroy you, but by the end I felt healed and happy. Kisa was a heroine that I loved. She had such strength and determination. She was willing to risk so much. These two characters were perfect together and both were survivors- so strong and resilient. They truly were a match. <br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%206/23569eec-7093-487d-b258-e7db698c7b27_zpsde205f32.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1420020397i/13154837.jpg" alt=" photo 23569eec-7093-487d-b258-e7db698c7b27_zpsde205f32.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>If it’s not obvious enough already, I will repeat it. This book is a must read. It’s just remarkable, exceptional, and completely extraordinary. Be prepared to feel. Be prepared to hurt, to cry, to be moved beyond belief, to have your heart stop and to be consumed by this gorgeous and enthralling story. It’s been days since I’ve read and my heart still feels for these two. It’s an unforgettable read that I loved from start to finish! <br><i>
  <b>
    <blockquote>“I need you with me. I only feel at home with you.”</blockquote>
  </b>
</i><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%206/5e70f7ec-766c-4c51-ac4b-4c6d4dcbc802_zpsa4013888.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1420020397i/13154838.jpg" alt=" photo 5e70f7ec-766c-4c51-ac4b-4c6d4dcbc802_zpsa4013888.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/5edf5586-e123-4b65-aabc-e59743177fba_zpsf705ae1e.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1415095596i/11723915.jpg" alt=" photo 5edf5586-e123-4b65-aabc-e59743177fba_zpsf705ae1e.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/fbfe5257-5c23-4da3-b325-31eaf8f2110a_zpsd0802295.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1399922023i/9610271.jpg" alt=" photo fbfe5257-5c23-4da3-b325-31eaf8f2110a_zpsd0802295.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a></span>
  <a data-text-id="16247669084376646649" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Val ⚓️ Shameless Non-Snowflake ⚓️" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Val ⚓️ Shameless Non-Snowflake ⚓️" href="/user/show/11626803-val-shameless-non-snowflake">Val ⚓️ Shameless Non-Snowflake ⚓️</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1063327149" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15471540192115609300"><b><i>11/12/15: Re-Read for </i>Reap...<i>because I started it and was like "What fuckery is this again?" Need a refresher...</i></b><br/><br/><b>3 Predictable Stars</b><br/><br/>So I am definitely in the minority on this one.<br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1420931269ra/13293639.gif' width='500' height='250' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>While it was definitely a decent read, I just didn't love it. It was simply...<br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1420931269i/13293640.gif' width='450' height='449' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>...in my opinion anyway.<br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1420931269ra/13293641.gif' width='500' height='205' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Raze was hot. <br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1420931269ra/13293642.gif' width='500' height='421' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>But Kisa was kind of flat and boring in my opinion.<br/><br/>Much like this pencil. <br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1420931269ra/13293643.gif' width='500' height='243' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>She just kind of went along with whichever way the "wind" blew. <br/><br/>No matter who was blowing it. <br/><br/>Mainly though, the story was just too </span>
  <span id="freeText15471540192115609300" style="display:none"><b><i>11/12/15: Re-Read for </i>Reap...<i>because I started it and was like "What fuckery is this again?" Need a refresher...</i></b><br><br><b>3 Predictable Stars</b><br><br>So I am definitely in the minority on this one.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1420931269ra/13293639.gif" width="500" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>While it was definitely a decent read, I just didn't love it. It was simply...<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1420931269i/13293640.gif" width="450" height="449" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>...in my opinion anyway.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1420931269ra/13293641.gif" width="500" height="205" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Raze was hot. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1420931269ra/13293642.gif" width="500" height="421" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>But Kisa was kind of flat and boring in my opinion.<br><br>Much like this pencil. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1420931269ra/13293643.gif" width="500" height="243" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>She just kind of went along with whichever way the "wind" blew. <br><br>No matter who was blowing it. <br><br>Mainly though, the story was just too predictable. I knew how this thing was gonna end VERY early on, like less than 5% in. Sometimes that works for me and I don't mind, so long as the journey to <i>get</i> to that known ending is good. <br><br>But for the entirety of this story, instead of feeling like this:<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1420931269ra/13293644.gif" width="426" height="228" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>...or even like this...<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1420931269ra/13293645.gif" width="500" height="278" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I felt like this:<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1420931269i/13293646.jpg" width="400" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1420931269ra/13293647.gif" width="432" height="422" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1420931269ra/13293648.gif" width="500" height="288" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>In fact, because it <i>was</i> so predictable, I often felt my mind wandering a bit.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1420931269ra/13293649.gif" width="480" height="213" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>All in all, still a decent read. Just not my favorite thing from Ms. Cole. <br><br>XXXXXXXXXXXXXXXXXXXXXXXXXXXXXX<br><br><b>10 MORE DAYS!!!</b><br><br>XXXXXXXXXXXXXXXXXXXXXXXXXXXXXX<br><br>I want it so bad!<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1411583979ra/11251969.gif" width="225" height="193" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></span>

        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1062764214" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13102144806551749064"><b>*****FOUR STARS*****</b><br/>{BR with my Beautiful Bestie}<br/><br/><br/><a href='http://s1276.photobucket.com/user/tennyspa/media/15a566909a3a64bcdf75154583e8daaa_zps5da904f5.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1420091477i/13170283._SY540_.jpg' alt=' photo 15a566909a3a64bcdf75154583e8daaa_zps5da904f5.jpg' width='365' height='400' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/><br/><br/>Fighter 818 has lived in the dark and hellish Gulag prison since he was a young teenage boy. Forced to fight in Death Matches and being pumped full of drugs to bulk him up and fill him with rage. Electric shock therapy has also been forced upon him to make him lose the memories of whom he once was. He's had one purpose running through his mind that kept him going and it was etched on his prison cell wall.<br/><br/><br/><br/><b>Alik Durov. Brooklyn, New York. Revenge</b></span>
  <span id="freeText13102144806551749064" style="display:none"><b>*****FOUR STARS*****</b><br>{BR with my Beautiful Bestie}<br><br><br><a href="http://s1276.photobucket.com/user/tennyspa/media/15a566909a3a64bcdf75154583e8daaa_zps5da904f5.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1420091477i/13170283._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo 15a566909a3a64bcdf75154583e8daaa_zps5da904f5.jpg" width="365" height="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br><br>Fighter 818 has lived in the dark and hellish Gulag prison since he was a young teenage boy. Forced to fight in Death Matches and being pumped full of drugs to bulk him up and fill him with rage. Electric shock therapy has also been forced upon him to make him lose the memories of whom he once was. He's had one purpose running through his mind that kept him going and it was etched on his prison cell wall.<br><br><br><br><b>Alik Durov. Brooklyn, New York. Revenge. Kill</b><br><br><br><br><br>All he knows is that this is the man who falsely accused him of murder and who is the reason he was sent to the Gulag. He plans to fight against Alik in a death match at The Dungeon, and this is where he will get his revenge.<br><br><br><br><br>Kisa Volkova is the daughter of the Pakhan, the top boss of the Bratva Russian Mafia. She is engaged to the man Fighter 818 is out to kill. She is trapped in a very abusive relationship and every day is haunted by the memories of the beautiful boy she loved with all her heart. A boy named Luka Tolstoi, who was the only son of one of the Bratva kings. Everyone thinks he died when he was 14, in a bus accident, but turns out, he's the guy out for revenge against Kisa's fiance.<br><br><br><br><br><br>The two will meet in a dark alley where Kisa is handing out meals to homeless people for her Church that she does volunteer work for. 818 aka RAZE comes to her rescue as she is about to be attacked by a robber. Kisa and Raze have an instant connection. Something about his eyes is so familiar to her.<br><br><br><br><br><br>They manage to get some stolen moments together and Kisa soon figures out that Raze is her one and only love, Luka. He sees her in his dreams but has trouble putting things all together in his head. When the sexy times finally happen, let me just say it is heartbreaking and then soon it is incredibly steamy. We find out some things that happened to Luka that just ripped my heart apart.<br><br><br><br><br><br>This book had a lot of extremely violent scenes and there was one in particular that had me praying for a slow and painful death for Alik. But there was also a beautiful love story in here too. A story about two people who were made for each other. Whose souls would find each other no matter what.<br><br><br><br><br><i>
  <b>"You can have me, solnyshko. You can have all of me. You always have, and you always will."</b>
</i><br><br><br><br><br>I really enjoyed this one but something was missing. I can't really place my finger on it. Was it predictable? Yes. But it was still entertaining. The only other thing that I had a problem with was the Epilogue. My Bestie pointed out that it was too short. It felt rushed. We would have liked to see where Kisa and Luka are at years later, but we didn't get that insight.<br><br><br></span>
  <a data-text-id="13102144806551749064" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_1147203133" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1147203133" />
    <a title="Lady Vigilante (Feifei)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2551178-lady-vigilante-feifei"><img alt="Lady Vigilante (Feifei)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1421992465p2/2551178.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1147203133?book_show_action=true">Dec 30, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Lady Vigilante (Feifei)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Lady Vigilante (Feifei)" href="/user/show/2551178-lady-vigilante-feifei">Lady Vigilante (Feifei)</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2551178-lady-vigilante-feifei?shelf=i-trust-my-friends">i-trust-my-friends</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2551178-lady-vigilante-feifei?shelf=contemporary-duckie">contemporary-duckie</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2551178-lady-vigilante-feifei?shelf=choke-dat-ho">choke-dat-ho</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2551178-lady-vigilante-feifei?shelf=panty-dropping-hot">panty-dropping-hot</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2551178-lady-vigilante-feifei?shelf=alpha-heroes">alpha-heroes</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2551178-lady-vigilante-feifei?shelf=dark-reads">dark-reads</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2551178-lady-vigilante-feifei?shelf=pull-out-the-guns-mafia">pull-out-the-guns-mafia</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1147203133" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3136387729594525832"><b>4 stars!</b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1420063383i/13162872._SX540_.jpg' width='400' height='375' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Even though this is only the second book I’ve read from Tillie Cole, I can already see what a versatile writer she is. I mean this in a good way but never in a million years did I expect the author of <u>Sweet Fall</u> – a highly emotional and poignant NA romance – to come up with a gritty and twisted mafia romance like this one. Though there were a few hiccups along the way, this book was <b>INTENSE</b> from start to finish. There is something special about this author’s writing that is just gripping</span>
  <span id="freeText3136387729594525832" style="display:none"><b>4 stars!</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1420063383i/13162872._SX540_.jpg" width="400" height="375" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Even though this is only the second book I’ve read from Tillie Cole, I can already see what a versatile writer she is. I mean this in a good way but never in a million years did I expect the author of <u>Sweet Fall</u> – a highly emotional and poignant NA romance – to come up with a gritty and twisted mafia romance like this one. Though there were a few hiccups along the way, this book was <b>INTENSE</b> from start to finish. There is something special about this author’s writing that is just gripping and makes the book unputdownable. On top of that, there’s this hidden element to the romance that’ll be revealed early on in the story that just made my heart RACE. I was rooting for these characters hard!<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1420063383i/13162873._SX540_.jpg" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Number 818 or ‘Raze’ is taken from his home when he was a young boy and then raised and brainwashed into a cold-blooded killing machine in the fighting rings, where one fights to kill. He doesn’t remember much about his past because of the drugs fed to him, only that he has one purpose: to get revenge on the man who wrongly accused him of a crime he didn’t commit. His search leads him to the heart of a ruthless death match enterprise and straight into the path of a blue-eyed girl whose face is eerily similar to the girl in his fuzzy memories.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1420063383i/13162874._SY540_.jpg" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Kisa Volkova is the daughter of the man who runs a savage underground fighting ring and betrothed to the long-time champion, a demented and truly twisted man who’s obsessed with possessing her. She’s well aware that in this mafia life, she has little say in what she wants and is physically and emotionally battered by her fiancé’s demands and the invisible iron cage her family has her own. Fully knowing that her heart belongs to another – a man she has never seen again since her childhood – Kisa has resolved herself to become the dutiful wife everyone in the mafia expects her to be.<br><br>On one fateful night, Kisa is saved from an unknown assailant by Raze, who’s come to the city to get his revenge against Alik Durov, who’s also Kisa’s fiancé. Without spoiling anything, Kisa and Raze have this insanely intense connection and can’t help but be drawn towards each other, even though their attraction is the last thing they need with Kisa already engaged to another and Raze only interested in his revenge plan.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1420063383i/13162875._SX540_.jpg" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>The first half of this book left me breathless. My heart was pounding from the fight scenes, the sizzling chemistry between Kisa and Raze, and the hidden element to their romance that gave my heart a squeeze. I just wanted them to be together without any obstacles in their way, you know? But their road was not an easy one, and I’m glad the author made it bumpy or else it really would’ve cheapened their romance. I think my main concern with this book was the big discrepancy between the first and second halves of the story. It seemed too convenient that <i>every</i> problem Raze had (from his memory loss to revenge plan etc…) was wrapped up and concluded so nicely. The first half of the book really set a gritty and challenging pace for these characters and though I’m sure it wasn’t the author’s intention, I felt like the second half of the book got a little too cheesy and predictable. Nevertheless, my overall enjoyment of this story was high, and I could overlook these things because I was invested in the romance and genuinely cared about the characters’ welfare.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1420063383i/13162876._SX540_.jpg" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>By the time I got to the end of the book, I was sad the story was ending and wished there was more. I love the mafia world the author set up and strangely enough, there were two side characters I loved just as much (maybe even a little more) than Kisa and Raze and whether or not it’ll happen, I wish the author could do books for them too: Rodion (Kisa’s brother) and fighter number 362 (Raze’s rival and friend). All in all, this story had my attention from beginning to end, got me invested in these characters, and had me wishing there was more to the story after it ended…which I think are all essential aspects that comprise a good book. I couldn’t be happier to end my 2014 reading year on a high note! <br><br><u>Raze</u> is a dark contemporary romance set in the mafia world. It’s a true standalone and unrelated to the author’s other books.</span>
  <a data-text-id="3136387729594525832" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<span id="freeTextContainer11714163837435803434">I'm not usually a romance fan. I can read them and sometimes I get a wild hair up my butt and even search them out. This book was being read by most of my romance fan friends and it caught my attention.<br/><br/>I'm actually glad it did. It's actually some pretty dark stuff...and of course I liked it. <br/><br/>818 aka Raze was thrown into a prison at a young age. That sounds not so bad doesn't it? Bullshit. He is raped, tortured, injected with drugs and made to fight to the death..over 600 times.<br/>He has no memories</span>
  <span id="freeText11714163837435803434" style="display:none">I'm not usually a romance fan. I can read them and sometimes I get a wild hair up my butt and even search them out. This book was being read by most of my romance fan friends and it caught my attention.<br><br>I'm actually glad it did. It's actually some pretty dark stuff...and of course I liked it. <br><br>818 aka Raze was thrown into a prison at a young age. That sounds not so bad doesn't it? Bullshit. He is raped, tortured, injected with drugs and made to fight to the death..over 600 times.<br>He has no memories of his previous life due to the huge amounts of brutality he faced. <br>Then he escapes. He wants revenge on a name that has been written in his cell for years because he was told he would forget if it wasn't written there.<br><br>Then for the girl. Kisa. She is a Russian mafia princess who is engaged to a major and I do mean major asshole. She has no escape from him due to family traditions (you do not go against this family)<br>Kisa's side of the story almost got this book a 3 star from me. She is supposed to be this classy chick and her side of the story doesn't read as so much class to me. (not that I'm a saint) Her inner dialogue has when she um gets worked up with the guy she keeps saying how her pussy is wet. Ewww. What woman does that inside her head? We don't really use that word for that.<br> <a href="http://imgur.com/MyYP58q" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1420142261ra/13179983.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>For the guys side of the story it worked fine because these are some hard fuckers..I mean some of the most hardened guys out there.<br>Her fiance Alik? He needs his balls kicked in. Multiple times.<br><a href="http://imgur.com/1ZODhZf" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1420142261ra/13179984.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>I did give this book a four star though. Because once I started reading it I wanted to keep reading it...and it did make this cold heart melt at times.<br><a href="http://imgur.com/NyFleFb" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1420142261ra/13179985.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Romance fan friends-I'm watching you. You guys might just be on to something.<br><br><br>P.S. this book has some raunchy ass sex scenes...not that I read those parts four times or not.</span>

<div id="review_1102590393" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1102590393" />
    <a title="Brandi" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5494655-brandi"><img alt="Brandi" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1384348451p2/5494655.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1102590393?book_show_action=true">Nov 10, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Brandi" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Brandi" href="/user/show/5494655-brandi">Brandi</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5494655-brandi?shelf=suspense">suspense</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5494655-brandi?shelf=dark-twisty">dark-twisty</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1102590393" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9393399593542911991"><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1420036913i/13157449._SY540_.jpg' width='400' height='400' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Holy hell. I don't even know where to start. This book was OTT and predictable, BUT I really liked it. I don't know why, but it was addictive. Seriously, I couldn't put it down. <br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1420036913i/13157450._SY540_.jpg' width='400' height='487' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>818 aka Raze has no memory of his life before the Gulag - the hell he has lived in, forced to fight to the death for as long as he can remember. The only thing that keeps him going are the words carved into his cell wall.<br/><br/><i>
  <b>Alik Durov. <br/>Brooklyn, New York. <br/>Revenge. <br/>Kill.</b>
</i><br/><br/>Kisa Volkova is a Russian mod princess, engaged to </span>
  <span id="freeText9393399593542911991" style="display:none"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1420036913i/13157449._SY540_.jpg" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Holy hell. I don't even know where to start. This book was OTT and predictable, BUT I really liked it. I don't know why, but it was addictive. Seriously, I couldn't put it down. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1420036913i/13157450._SY540_.jpg" width="400" height="487" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>818 aka Raze has no memory of his life before the Gulag - the hell he has lived in, forced to fight to the death for as long as he can remember. The only thing that keeps him going are the words carved into his cell wall.<br><br><i>
  <b>Alik Durov. <br>Brooklyn, New York. <br>Revenge. <br>Kill.</b>
</i><br><br>Kisa Volkova is a Russian mod princess, engaged to a psychopath, she lives a sheltered life under the constant control of Alik. One night while volunteering for the church, she is attacked and saved by a mysterious man. She knows she must stay away from him, but something about him calls to her and she can't resist. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1420037240i/13157473._SY540_.jpg" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I won't go into the story too much more, I don't want to spoil anything. <i>Raze</i> was an interesting, fast-paced, steamy romance. While a bit ridiculous, I enjoyed it. </span>

<div id="review_1139531417" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1139531417" />
    <a title="Lana ❇✾DG Romance❇✾" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5498948-lana-dg-romance"><img alt="Lana ❇✾DG Romance❇✾" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1376622739p2/5498948.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1139531417?book_show_action=true">Dec 23, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Lana ❇✾DG Romance❇✾" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Lana ❇✾DG Romance❇✾" href="/user/show/5498948-lana-dg-romance">Lana ❇✾DG Romance❇✾</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5498948-lana-dg-romance?shelf=dark-read">dark-read</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5498948-lana-dg-romance?shelf=part-of-a-series">part-of-a-series</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5498948-lana-dg-romance?shelf=scarred-hero">scarred-hero</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5498948-lana-dg-romance?shelf=erotic">erotic</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5498948-lana-dg-romance?shelf=erotic-romance">erotic-romance</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1139531417" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1786135631688616489"><b>2.5 Stars</b><br/><img src='https://s3.amazonaws.com/photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1446422768r/16804581.jpg?v=1446422770250' width='400' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380397315i/766520.png' width='50' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>He was as cold as an arctic winter... but he was a beautiful monster...</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1408067509ra/10803442.gif' width='400' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/>After so many friends raved to me about how amazing this book was, I was beyond excited to be finally reading it. Given that I've also spent quite a few months avoiding it. Why? Because my picky Russian ass has yet to read a book with the MCs being Russian and not having it be butchered to hell and back. So I get a little touchy. <br/><br/>I have to say, I was very impressed with the way the author accurately portr</span>
  <span id="freeText1786135631688616489" style="display:none"><b>2.5 Stars</b><br><img src="https://s3.amazonaws.com/photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1446422768r/16804581.jpg?v=1446422770250" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380397315i/766520.png" width="50" class="gr-hostedUserImg">He was as cold as an arctic winter... but he was a beautiful monster...</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1408067509ra/10803442.gif" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>After so many friends raved to me about how amazing this book was, I was beyond excited to be finally reading it. Given that I've also spent quite a few months avoiding it. Why? Because my picky Russian ass has yet to read a book with the MCs being Russian and not having it be butchered to hell and back. So I get a little touchy. <br><br>I have to say, I was very impressed with the way the author accurately portrayed the Bratva and the true brutal underbelly of it. The concept and the story were intriguing, violent, intense, and gripping. The book kept my attention the entire time reading it. But unfortunately there were too many issues that I had along with it that ultimately killed my buzz.<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1431112387ra/14793324.gif" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Be warned....nitpicking galore to follow...<br><br><b> The character's names.</b><br>First we have Kisa. But here's the thing; I've never heard of a name like this in Russian. Ever. It <b>is</b> a very common term of endearment however. It loosely translates to "pussy cat" or "kitten". Whatever your fancy. But here's the issue, Kisa's fiance likes to call her "Myshka", which translates to 'little mouse'.<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1392241179i/8524698._SY540_.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Yeah. Threw me too.<br><br><b> The writing.</b><br>OK look, I know I'm picky here but this just didn't work for me in the least. I found some parts of the book to be choppy. It goes from incredibly emotional and gritty to borderline cheesy. <br>Like this phrase here:<br><b>"Please, sit, papas."</b><br>Why on earth would someone say, "Please, sit, fathers"? Unless you're in church. But again, that's neither here nor there. My main issue came with the dialogue, internal and external. The repetitive terminology, especially within the character's dialogue managed to frustrate me enough to take me out of the story at times.<br>The overuse of endearments and names within one paragraph being my main issue. I get it; she's your Myshka, your Solnyshko, and he's tvoya lyubov. I just don't want it repeated ad nauseam, feel me?<br><br>Also, in Russian culture you never refer to someone respectfully especially of authority by their first name. So you would never call your employer <b>Mr. Alik.</b> You'd refer to him by his first and middle name, so Alik Abramovich in the case here. But again, that's neither here nor there.<br><br><b> The heroine</b> Nothing about Kisa worked for me. She was bland to the point of blending in with the furniture. There was nothing about her that grabbed me as a reader or endeared me. She was weak and her simple acceptance of things just being what they are and such is life did nothing for me either. Don't get me started on her vagina's pavlov response to the mere presence of Raze. The woman would walk into a room, see his back without knowing it's him, and already she's raring to go?<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1446426853ra/16805859.gif" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Taking into consideration her borderline abusive psycho of a fiancé and their relationship, I'm shocked she had no emotional or mental scars. This is especially true towards the end. She moves on from all of it without so much as a bat of a eye lash. No lingering emotional trauma...just is what it is.<br><br><b>The overuse of the word "channel</b><br>Perhaps this is just me, but I have never once referred to my southern region as a "channel" during internal monologue during sex. So the fact the Kisa thinks how her <i>clenching channel wrapped around his cock</i> made me wonder if perhaps she was a victorian maiden in her past life.<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1446426853ra/16805860.gif" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>The overuse of endearments</b><br>Considering the gritty and brutal subject matter of this book, I can understand why the author would want to dilute that with a beautiful love story. However, I just can't picture any person in their late 20s referring to the other as "my love" on a constant and consistent basis. I'm talking about multiple times during one sex scene. Perhaps it's my inner cynic kicking in, but this was just too much cheese for me.<br><br><b>The graphic sex scenes with Kisa's fiance</b><br>I'm not a reader that has an issue of a graphic sex scene with a person that's not the main love interest in a romance. Especially not when it fits the plot as it did here. That being said, it didn't need to be as often or as graphic as it was here. After the first time, I didn't see a reason for it. Yes, I get it, Alik is brutal and sadisctic. He feels that Kisa is his property and he goes absolutely batshit at another man so much as looking at her. I do NOT want to be reading about this more than I need to which was for basically <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[over half the book <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>. Did it fit the plot? Sure. Could it have been toned down? Absolutely.<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1412877994ra/11435626.gif" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>It could have easily been fade to black or just loosely mentioned. It simply didn't need to be as graphic as it was past the first 2 times.<br><br>Having said all that, the story itself was unique and gripping enough to have me turning the pages. Sure it was a little predictable in places but I don't think it was ever really meant to be a huge secret. I didn't see a good part of the ending coming, so in terms of suspense and grit, it certainly fit the bill. Raze was the star of the book. I couldn't help but fall for him right away. The violence was graphic and at times extremely difficult to read. But at the same time, it just didn't effect me as much as some of the other gritty and dark books I read. While this may not have completely worked for me, I'm intrigued enough to continue with the series. Hopefully with the next book being traditionally published, some of the issues I had here may be ironed out.<br><br><i>ARC courtesy of publisher in exchange for an honest review</i><br><br><b>For more reviews visit<br><a href="http://dirtygirlromance.com" target="blogspot" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1436477285i/15465455._SX540_.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a></b></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>
  <a data-text-id="1786135631688616489" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_1147491613" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1147491613" />
    <a title="Beverly" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/13095060-beverly"><img alt="Beverly" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1466964369p2/13095060.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1147491613?book_show_action=true">Dec 30, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Beverly" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Beverly" href="/user/show/13095060-beverly">Beverly</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1147491613" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer836803185099329001"><b>5 <i>Raze Haze</i> Stars</b><br/><br/>I couldn’t be more blown away with this beautiful, heartbreaking story. It begins as one thing and then completely transitions into another, both sides had me completely captivated.<br/><br/>When things begin we learn of an underground fight ring. The boys, yes boys – not men, fighting in these fights are not fighting for money, but something much more precious, their lives. This is where we meet fighter 818. He is the undefeated fighter at his camp. When the fighters rebel and cause a ri</span>
  <span id="freeText836803185099329001" style="display:none"><b>5 <i>Raze Haze</i> Stars</b><br><br>I couldn’t be more blown away with this beautiful, heartbreaking story. It begins as one thing and then completely transitions into another, both sides had me completely captivated.<br><br>When things begin we learn of an underground fight ring. The boys, yes boys – not men, fighting in these fights are not fighting for money, but something much more precious, their lives. This is where we meet fighter 818. He is the undefeated fighter at his camp. When the fighters rebel and cause a riot 818 is able to escape. He has been drugged, abused and taught to kill; he doesn’t remember his name, where he is from or his family. The only thing he knows is his desire for revenge - he must kill Alik Durov.<br><br>Alik Durov is the heir to the Bratva family and a lethal fighter. He is engaged to his family friend and the female heir, Kisa. Alik is a horrible man who enjoys hurting others, he is mentally unstable and abusive to Kisa. Despite Kisa’s fears of Alik she does what she was raised to do: be a good Bratva woman. She isn’t in love Alik, but loves him in a friendly way. She knows he needs her and is scared for him to be without her. Kisa’s one true love was her childhood friend and boyfriend Luka, but Luka is gone.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1420592308i/13242856._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>A lot of people find Kisa’s demeanor and attitude to be frustrating, but I get her. She was raised to be a certain way and lost her true love a long time ago. She knows no matter what she will never love another like she did Luka, so she will be the woman she was raised to be. A lot of people think it is weakness that keeps her in her situation, but I think it takes great strength to sacrifice yourself for the ones you love. <br><br>Once she meets Raze everything changes. She sees something in him and wants to help him. There is something about him she can’t turn away from.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1420592308i/13242857._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I don’t want to spoil this book for anyone, so I will stop there. This story brought out so many emotions in me and had me thinking about it nonstop. It begins dark and transitions into one of the most beautiful love stories. I loved watching things unfold and seeing the compassion, desire, and protectiveness between these characters. I was on the edge of my seat reading this one and couldn’t wait to turn the page, then when I got to the end I was devastated it was over. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1420592308i/13242858._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Tillie Cole has quickly become one of my favorite authors. I truly believe she can write anything, her writing always evokes such strong emotions in me. Her stories are well written and she creates unforgettable characters. I always find myself completely enthralled and cheering for them. As much as I love all her stories, I think Raze is my favorite. There was just something about this story that hooked me. When I say I was in a Raze Haze it was legit, I couldn’t stop thinking about this beautiful story of two broken people hell bent on healing each other. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1420592308i/13242859._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></span>
  <a data-text-id="836803185099329001" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Flo" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Flo" href="/user/show/7643503-flo">Flo</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7643503-flo?shelf=contemporary-romance">contemporary-romance</a>,

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7643503-flo?shelf=standalone">standalone</a>,

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7643503-flo?shelf=best-of-2016">best-of-2016</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1146110275" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15806714291660118308"><b>5 **<u>star-crossed</u>** STARS</b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1451906085i/17619071.png' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“You're a part of me, remember? God put a piece of you within me so when we were born, everyone would know we matched.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br/><br/>All I have to say is...what took me so long? I’m way late to the party and there are no excuses. This book was fantastic from start to finish. Just my kind of book. A revenge and mob story, about two soul mates and the cruelty they had to endure until they could find each other <a class='jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction'>(view spoiler)</a><span class='spoilerContainer' style='display: none'>[again <a class='jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction'>(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>. Beautiful, heartbreaking, gr</span>
  <span id="freeText15806714291660118308" style="display:none"><b>5 **<u>star-crossed</u>** STARS</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1451906085i/17619071.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“You're a part of me, remember? God put a piece of you within me so when we were born, everyone would know we matched.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>All I have to say is...what took me so long? I’m way late to the party and there are no excuses. This book was fantastic from start to finish. Just my kind of book. A revenge and mob story, about two soul mates and the cruelty they had to endure until they could find each other <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[again <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>. Beautiful, heartbreaking, gripping and spellbinding. Perfect. Like it was written with my taste in mind. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1418911509i/12944326.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“I’m closing my eyes so I can feel being inside you.” He placed his hand over his heart and rasped out, “I’ve seen too many bad things with these eyes. This, I will feel in my heart.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br><b>818</b>, also called Raze has escaped hell, the gulag where he had been prisoner since he was a boy. Trained to be a fighter, tortured, abused and brainwashed. A monster with only one directive...kill. He knows nothing of who he was before he got there, only one name, address and the word revenge carved into his cell. So this is what he sets out to do, find the man and get revenge. Because it is the only thing he has left.<br><br>Raze is such a <a>Tillie Cole</a> character. If you have read the <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/series/128581-hades-hangmen" rel="nofollow noopener">Hades Hangmen</a> series you probably know what I'm talking about. He is a one man army, brutal and damaged. Broken beyond recognition, but in no way a bad person. Ms. Cole has a way of writing these complex and vulnerable heroes who have a rough exterior, pain in their hearts and yet turn out to be the most genuine and gentle souls. Someone you have to feel deeply for and eventually fall in love with.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1451913791i/17620597.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Kisa Volkova</b> is the daughter of Kirill Volkov, the boss of New York's Russian Bratva. She is sheltered and protected, but her life is more like being trapped in a deathly golden cage than anything else. Her fiancé being one of the most dangerous things in her life, and all that takes a turn for the worst and the best at the same time, the night she meets Raze. Once their paths cross nothing will ever be the same again.<br><br>Kisa is the epitome of strength. You can tell she is russian and groomed to be a mafia wife. There is very little that faces her on the outside. She has coping mechanisms most people would kill for. But really the most interesting thing happens when Kisa and Raze connect. It's beautiful and tragic and raw. Really a once in a lifetime love story.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1418911509i/12944326.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“You can have me, solnyshko. You can have all of me. You always have, and you always will.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>What else can I say? I love <i>Tillie Cole</i> and her dark and gritty books never cease to capture me. Her writing sucks you in, makes you feel all the feels, sends your emotions on a rollercoaster ride, makes you hide in fear and in the end ments your heart with beautiful love. Can you tell I loved this book? <br><br>Well here is the thing. This is the kind of genre and set up that gets my blood flowing. Revenge, copious amounts of violence, raw chemistry that quite literally jumps off the page, wonderfully damaged characters, with a little mystery and danger sprinkled on top. My kind of book. No two ways about it.<br><br>And FYI, since I'm so hooked and obsessed with this right now, I already started <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/25732126-reap" rel="nofollow noopener">Reap</a>, book 2 in the Scarred Souls series...good news, Kisa and Raze's story gets some page time next to the main couple. <br><br>That's all. Thank you for your time. ;)<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1418911509i/12944326.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><a href="http://coffeeaddictbooks.blogspot.co.at/" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1447539995i/17017465.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><a href="https://www.facebook.com/coffeeaddictbooks?ref=tn_tnmn" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1431598100i/14852514.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> <a href="https://twitter.com/flo_reads" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1431598236i/14852521.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> <a href="http://coffeeaddictbooks.blogspot.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1431598236i/14852522.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">

<div id="review_1061824919" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1061824919" />
    <a title="✦❋Arianna✦❋" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/23370948-arianna"><img alt="✦❋Arianna✦❋" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1420671997p2/23370948.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1061824919?book_show_action=true">Sep 22, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="✦❋Arianna✦❋" class="user" itemprop="url" name="✦❋Arianna✦❋" href="/user/show/23370948-arianna">✦❋Arianna✦❋</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/23370948-arianna?shelf=dark-romance">dark-romance</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1061824919" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15619482609954514586"><b>4 Stars!!</b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1447166571i/16965251.jpg' width='400' height='350' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>I have read many books from Tillie Cole, but none of them was like this one for me. I’m a sucker for dark, gritty and twisted reads and this romance mafia was all this and more. To say I’m glad I finally give this book a try would be an understatement. If you haven’t read this book yet my advice is to consider reading it ASAP. This story didn’t disappoint. It was gripping from start to finish even if at times it was a little rushed and predictable. The writing was flawless and the hero </span>
  <span id="freeText15619482609954514586" style="display:none"><b>4 Stars!!</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1447166571i/16965251.jpg" width="400" height="350" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I have read many books from Tillie Cole, but none of them was like this one for me. I’m a sucker for dark, gritty and twisted reads and this romance mafia was all this and more. To say I’m glad I finally give this book a try would be an understatement. If you haven’t read this book yet my advice is to consider reading it ASAP. This story didn’t disappoint. It was gripping from start to finish even if at times it was a little rushed and predictable. The writing was flawless and the hero a damaged man you will root for from the start. <br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“From now on, you’ll be known as fighter 818, and if you want to live, you’ll learn how to fight and how to survive here, in hell.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>Number 818 (Raze) was taken since he was only a young boy to a place where he became a cold killer, a killing machine, a fighter who not only fights for entertainment, but fights to stay alive. Kill or be killed. That’s how Number 818 lived since he remembers. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1447166571i/16965252.jpg" width="400" height="405" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>His brain was shut down blocking out anything but the need to kill, erasing his knowledge of who he is and where he is from. He knows only one thing – that he must get revenge on Alik Durov. For what exactly? He doesn’t remember, but he knows and he feels this man wronged him like no one else. And he will find him and he would kill him no matter what. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1447166571i/16965253.jpg" width="400" height="475" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Kisa Volkova is a Russian Mafiya princess. Her father is one of the three “Red” Bratva Kings in New York, the top boss, the one who rules the Russian underground in the city. Her fiancée is a sick, twisted, possessive man who controls almost everything in her life. She knows very well her role as the Pakhan’s daughter and the fiancée of the best death match fighter Bratva has. Even if she ‘has enough time’ to fall for her fiancée, she never forgot her first true love. <br><br>Kisa and Raze meet when Raze saves her from being raped and possibly killed. They part ways, but they meet again when Raze comes to fight for Kisa’s father in order to be close to his target, Kisa’s fiancée Alik Durov. Even if both of them know they should stay away from each other for different reasons, they are drawn to the other immediately. Something starts between them, something that could destroy them.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1447166571i/16965254.jpg" width="400" height="475" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I enjoyed this one more than I expected. It wasn’t my first Mafia romance and certainly it won’t be my last, but I have to say this book surprised me in a very good way. Tillie Cole did a fantastic job portraying The Bratva World. The story not only was gripping, but was gritty and intense as well. The first half of the story was fast paced which I loved and kept me at the edge of my seat multiple times. The second half was more sweet and emotional and at times maybe a little OTT and cheesy, but I enjoyed it as well. Like I mentioned before, the story was predictable, but the execution was pretty good. There were also a few times when everything was a little too convenient for my taste. <br><br>I liked the hero, Raze. He was for sure an intriguing man and IMO his character was better developed than Kisa’s. I really felt for this broken man and I fell for him from the start. Kisa was just an ok character for me. She felt a little flat and there were times when she really annoyed me. Raze and Kisa’s connection was fantastically done and their sexy times were sweet and/or sexy and intimate. <br><br>Overall, this one was an entertaining read and I’m looking forward to read the next installments in the series. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1447166572i/16965255.jpg" width="400" height="350" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> </span>
  <a data-text-id="15619482609954514586" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_1062108268" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1062108268" />
    <a title="Patrycja" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/6852653-patrycja"><img alt="Patrycja" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1586460589p2/6852653.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1062108268?book_show_action=true">Sep 23, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Patrycja" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Patrycja" href="/user/show/6852653-patrycja">Patrycja</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>
