        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1062108268" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15135637348619189625"><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1391618077i/8420433._SX540_.jpg' width='400' height='40' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>Title:</b> 	Raze<br/><b>Series:</b> Standalone<br/><b>Author:</b> Tillie Cole<br/><b>Release Date: </b> December 30, 2014<br/><b>Rating:</b> 4.5 stars<br/><b>Cliffhanger:</b>. No<br/><b> HEA: </b> <a class='jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction'>(view spoiler)</a><span class='spoilerContainer' style='display: none'>[ Yes  <a class='jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction'>(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1391618077i/8420434._SX540_.jpg' width='400' height='40' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><br/>Every new book Tillie Cole releases is a thrilling ride. I am never sure what exactly will I get; Tillie can so wonderfully mix sweet with dark and you just never know if it will be sweet and charming swoony story or gritty and heartbreaking ride. With Raze the situation seemed simple, I excepted dark, I knew it would be dark and controversi</span>
  <span id="freeText15135637348619189625" style="display:none"><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1391618077i/8420433._SX540_.jpg" width="400" height="40" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Title:</b> 	Raze<br><b>Series:</b> Standalone<br><b>Author:</b> Tillie Cole<br><b>Release Date: </b> December 30, 2014<br><b>Rating:</b> 4.5 stars<br><b>Cliffhanger:</b>. No<br><b> HEA: </b> <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ Yes  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1391618077i/8420434._SX540_.jpg" width="400" height="40" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br>Every new book Tillie Cole releases is a thrilling ride. I am never sure what exactly will I get; Tillie can so wonderfully mix sweet with dark and you just never know if it will be sweet and charming swoony story or gritty and heartbreaking ride. With Raze the situation seemed simple, I excepted dark, I knew it would be dark and controversial. And boy did I get it. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1419795418i/13127924.jpg" width="400" height="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Kisa and Raze’s story is no fairytale. </b>It’s more of a twisted nightmare. I If you cannot handle freaky stuff it may give you a serious heart attack. <b>This book is full of revenge, lust, hate and love. </b><br><br>Kisa is mafia princess. She’s stuck in a gruesome world of blood and power play. Being the daughter of Russian mafia’s king is brutal. She has to act in certain way and do things that she doesn’t want to do. Which includes being engaged to Alik. And Alik is horrible human being… Kisa’s strong character and I loved her. I was impressed with her ability to carry so much weight on her shoulders. Her life was rough. <br><br>Then there is Raze. He’s mostly known as a 818. A fighter. He was a slave. As just a boy he started fighting for his life and learning how to kill only to survive….<br><br><b>I killed because I had to. I had no other choice. I was already dead, no more than a number; stripped of morals, stripped of freedom and stripped of life. I was an animal conditioned to inflict pain without remorse. And you cannot kill someone who has no soul. </b><br><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1419795418i/13127925.jpg" width="400" height="500" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Sometimes I read books that make me silent; I just have no idea how to put in words how intense and moving the experience was. I don’t want to slip and write something that will destroy the book for others. So it’s mostly best of I keep my mouth shut; there are books that just have to be read without any additional knowledge and Raze is one of them. So I won’t be telling you more about the plot. <br><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1419795418i/13127926.jpg" width="400" height="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>This book is just so…. Gruesome and heart shattering and nothing like the rest I’ve ever read. It’s unique. Shocking. Painful. This story captivated me, shocked me, made me bite my nails, scream and cry. So yes you can say that once again I am mind blown by Tillie Cole’s ability to create.<br><br><i> ARC kindly provided by Tillie Cole in exchange for an honest review.</i><br><br><b>FOLLOW SMOKIN HOT   <i>"What the hell had happened to him? And where the hell had he come from?"</i>
</b><br/><br/><span>[image error]</span><br/> <br/>Tillie Cole brings fans a story about a Russian mafia princess and the two guys who claim her and her heart. The story has a lot of to the rape scenes and death cage fighting scenes in it so be warned. Kind of reminded me of this old show...<br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1491993657i/22470226.jpg' width='390' height='250' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/> <br/><br/>The story was fast paced, at times predictable but overall a good read as number 818/Raze escapes his prison with no memories of his life prior with just a name and pl</span>
  <span id="freeText876087642714550132" style="display:none"><br><b>
  <i>"What the hell had happened to him? And where the hell had he come from?"</i>
</b><br><br><span>[image error]</span><br> <br>Tillie Cole brings fans a story about a Russian mafia princess and the two guys who claim her and her heart. The story has a lot of to the rape scenes and death cage fighting scenes in it so be warned. Kind of reminded me of this old show...<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1491993657i/22470226.jpg" width="390" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>The story was fast paced, at times predictable but overall a good read as number 818/Raze escapes his prison with no memories of his life prior with just a name and place to seek his revenge on the person who destroyed his life. <br> <br>There were times I was confused as to why the heroine never just told her father the true abuse she lived because he would have had her back one hundred percent. I felt she had this martyr thing going for her when it concerned him. There were also times when Raze’s memories came back right on cue and the eye color connection was mention way too much for my tastes. The couple’s sex scenes were very intimate and realistic. <br><br><b>
  <i>”I’m closing my eyes so I can feel being inside you.” He placed his hand over his heart and rasped out. “I’ve seen too many bad things with these eyes. This, I will feel with my heart.”</i>
</b><br><br>I was very choked up at what happened to poor 362. So overall this was an entertaining read about souls finding their mates after being separated and wronged with just the right amount of revenge death match style.<br><br><b>
  <i>”You’re a part of me, remember? God put a piece of you within me so when we were born, everyone would know we matched.”</i>

<div id="review_1118978310" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1118978310" />
    <a title="Eda**" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/6285155-eda"><img alt="Eda**" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1581410351p2/6285155.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1118978310?book_show_action=true">Nov 30, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Eda**" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Eda**" href="/user/show/6285155-eda">Eda**</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6285155-eda?shelf=favourites">favourites</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1118978310" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9568389624817580148"><br/><b>
  <i>** 4,5-5 "<u>Can I have you?</u>" STARS **</i>
</b><br/><br/><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"Whatever our souls are made of, his and mine are the same."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br/>After seeing a <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/6185.Wuthering_Heights' title='Wuthering Heights by Emily Brontë' rel='nofollow noopener'>Wuthering Heights</a> quote in this book, which is my favorite book, always and forever, I knew I'd fall hopelessly in love with it. <i>This is the story of two lost souls finding and recognizing each other in the most unlikely places and finding their way back to love.</i> It is extraordinary, intense, raw, heartbreaking...simply <b>BEAUTIFUL!</b> I was still shedding bittersweet tears a </span>
  <span id="freeText9568389624817580148" style="display:none"><br><b>
  <i>** 4,5-5 "<u>Can I have you?</u>" STARS **</i>
</b><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"Whatever our souls are made of, his and mine are the same."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>After seeing a <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/6185.Wuthering_Heights" title="Wuthering Heights by Emily Brontë" rel="nofollow noopener">Wuthering Heights</a> quote in this book, which is my favorite book, always and forever, I knew I'd fall hopelessly in love with it. <i>This is the story of two lost souls finding and recognizing each other in the most unlikely places and finding their way back to love.</i> It is extraordinary, intense, raw, heartbreaking...simply <b>BEAUTIFUL!</b> I was still shedding bittersweet tears a few days after finishing it. I even dreamed about it one night!<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1400488979ra/9681966.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>You see, it's a story that grips you from the throat and doesn't let go for a while. <b>So be prepared.</b> Be prepared to cry. Be prepared to get choked-up. Be prepared to get obsessed. Because you won't be able put this book down once you flip the first page!<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1420660025ra/13248610.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>
  <u>Number 818 / Raze</u>
</b> doesn't know a life beyond the one in <i>Gulag</i>, his prison, his hell, the place in which he's been tortured and brainwashed, turned into a stone-cold killer, into <i>death itself</i>. The only thing he remembers about his past are the words carved into the wall of his cell:<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>Alik Durov. <br>Brooklyn, New York. <br>Revenge. <br>Kill.</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>Now he is free, thanks to his only friend, <b>
  <u>Number 362</u>
</b> and he can do the thing he promised himself years ago: He can kill the man that sent him to hell and return the favor, sending HIM into the pits of the real hell this time!<br><br><b>
  <u>Kisa Volkov</u>
</b> is the daughter of the Pakhan, aka the boss, of the <i>Bratva Russian Mafia</i> and one of the 3 most dangerous Mafia bosses in NY, the <i>Red Bratva Kings</i>. She is engaged to be married to <b>
  <u>Alik “The Butcher” Durov</u>
</b>, the five-time champion of the underground fight-to-death ring, <i>The Dungeon</i>, the sadistic, unforgiving, cruel and unhealthily obsessive death-match fighter everyone in New York is scared-to-death of. <i>But Kisa is still haunted by a pair of dark brown eyes, the left iris smudged with a small splash of blue. Eyes of a boy she has lost 12 years ago but could never let go of... <u><b>Luka Tolstoi</b></u>.</i><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“You’re a part of me, remember? God put a piece of you within me so when we were born, everyone would know we matched.”<br>~ LUKA</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1405079027ra/10336961.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>One night while distributing care packages to homeless people for the church, a burglar attacks Kisa for her purse and she is rescued by a mysterious huge homeless man with a gray sweatshirt with the hood pulled over his face. <i>There's something familiar about this man though...</i> Kisa can't understand the strange feelings this man evokes in her at first, but when his hood comes off and she loses herself in the depth of those dark brown eyes, <i><b>the same eyes of the boy Kisa has always been in love with</b>, she knows with all of her heart that her soulmate has finally returned to her...</i><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>I had never felt this before. Never felt this overwhelming lust, this consuming level of instant attraction... this raw and insatiable need to be with a man. It was DANGEROUS. It was HAUNTING. It was FORBIDDEN. And although it was so WRONG, <u>it felt so perfectly RIGHT.</u><br>~ KISA</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><u>Raze</u> was a wonderful man. My heart cracked every single time he felt lost and I cried for everything that he's been through. Seriously, his story will damage you. It will make your heart ache. <b>You will be amazed by how a man can be so strong, yet so vulnerable...</b><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“I'm closing my eyes so I can feel being inside you.” He placed his hand over his heart and rasped out, “I've seen too many bad things with these eyes. This, I will feel in my heart.”<br>~ RAZE</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><u>Alik Durov</u>, the motherf*cker... I hated him with passion! I wished him a <b>VERY</b> slow and painful death throughout the book and am so relieved by his ending.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1420660025ra/13248611.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>He somewhat reminded me of <b>“Crazy Frankie”</b> from <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/16109563.Undeniable__Undeniable___1_" title="Undeniable (Undeniable, #1) by Madeline Sheehan" rel="nofollow noopener">Undeniable</a> by Madeline Sheehan, but you see, I liked Frankie. He was a sicko too, but somehow he made me sympathize with him. Alik, on the other hand, rose no feelings of understanding in me at all. He was despicable and he should burn in f*ckin' hell!<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>LUKA: “You’re insane! You’re fucking sick in the head!”<br><br>ALIK: “Maybe, but she’s going to be mine. I want her. I need her. She calms me, and I’ll do anything to own her and have her all to myself and fucking away from you!”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>Lastly...<b>
  <u>Goliath</u>
</b>. You destroyed me, buddy.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1402437232ra/9937143.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>
  <u>My reason for the (-0,5) stars:</u>
</b> The fact that even after all that she's endured at the hands of Alik and learning about his sins, Kisa kept referring to Raze and Alik as <b>"her two loves"</b>, INFURIATED me! <b>Idiot.</b><br><br>This was my first <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/7074846.Tillie_Cole" title="Tillie Cole" rel="nofollow noopener">Tillie Cole</a> read and now that I'm reading her <b>Hades Hangmen</b> series too, I gotta say this author may end up in my Top 5 Authors list! There's something special about her writing that I can't quite put a finger on but feel it down to my bones nevertheless. I'll be reading anything that comes outta her pen from now on, that's a promise! ;)<br><br>///////////////<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“Can I have you?”<br><br>“You can have me, Solnyshko. You can have all of me. You always have, and you always will.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>///////////////<br><br></span>
  <a data-text-id="9568389624817580148" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_1156354504" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">

    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1156354504?book_show_action=true">Jan 04, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/24183939-raze">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13865261-pam?shelf=darkerside-mindfuckery">darkerside-mindfuckery</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13865261-pam?shelf=suspense-chills-n-thrills">suspense-chills-n-thrills</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13865261-pam?shelf=4">4</a>,

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13865261-pam?shelf=stand-alone">stand-alone</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1156354504" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6022651401117250060"><i>4.25 beautifully raw stars</i><br/><br/><b>
  <i>Raze. 818.</i>
</b><br/><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>818 became unrivaled. 818 became death. <br/><br/>A. Fucking. Stone. Cold. Killer.</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1421127825i/13326196.png' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Raze has been bidding his time; his time for revenge... he may not remember the reason for the revenge but he knows it is as much as a part of him as is the need to kill. When he was taken into hell for the first time, he had to learn quick how to survive, and that was to fight, to win and to kill. No regret, no remorse, not when the alternative is your own death. Pumped up</span>
  <span id="freeText6022651401117250060" style="display:none"><i>4.25 beautifully raw stars</i><br><br><b>
  <i>Raze. 818.</i>
</b><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>818 became unrivaled. 818 became death. <br><br>A. Fucking. Stone. Cold. Killer.</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1421127825i/13326196.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Raze has been bidding his time; his time for revenge... he may not remember the reason for the revenge but he knows it is as much as a part of him as is the need to kill. When he was taken into hell for the first time, he had to learn quick how to survive, and that was to fight, to win and to kill. No regret, no remorse, not when the alternative is your own death. Pumped up full of drugs, pushed to forget, he has one goal; <b>Alik Durov. Brooklyn, New York. Revenge. Kill.</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1421127825ra/13326197.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>
  <i>Kisa-Anna</i>
</b><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“My Kisa-Anna… my solnyshko… God put a piece of your blue eyes in mine so we would always know we matched…”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1421127825i/13326198.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Kisa-Anna was settled into her fate, a future that has been planned for her, a future that she has to dutifully follow. With nothing else to do but follow, she lives each day as if it were a punishment, not knowing it could be any different. After all being the daughter of one of the three "Red" Bratva Kings of New York, there is no place she can escape to, except the church. At church she finds a few moments of freedom and peace, and at church does she meet the man who would be her savior and the answer to her prayers. <br><blockquote>
  <i>“They were always meant to be together, one boy and one girl, two hearts split into two, sent to far-off lands on their own. For God wanted to see if true love could be tested. He wanted to see if two halves of one soul could find each other again, even against the odds. Years would pass, they would both be hurt, they would both be sad, but one day, when they least expected it, they would stumble into each other’s paths. The question is: would they recognize each other’s soul? Would they find their way back to love…?”</i>
</blockquote><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1421127825ra/13326199.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Raze</b> was a heartbreakingly gritty story about how truly fucked up the world can be, proving that no matter how much money you have, you can't buy happiness. This was one story I bought on impulse, the description intrigued me, the cover sold me, so suffice to say I had no clue what I was getting into. It was painful to read some parts because you just wanted to reach out do something but you are just a bystander watching and waiting. I can see how this wouldn't be a book for everyone, it's not a sugar coated, it's not pretty but it is sweet, beautifully raw and satisfying in all ways. <br><br>I went through the e-Motions, I hated how she honored her family's wishes, I would like to think that if I was in her case, I would fight or choose a different path, but with the dynamics of how much of her life was her family, accepting to her fate no matter how much it pained me to do so. I was in shock and in disgust every time Alik was on the page, that man was a true monster. And Raze, he is an unconventional hero, even thought what he had to do to survive was wrong, you couldn't help but wish him to survive. All the lies, the deceit, and the heartache...it was so sad. I loved the concept of how God put a piece of her in him so that their souls would find one another, it was beautiful, but it was a bit over-done at the same time, encountering it all throughout the book. I would definitely recommend this read, especially if your looking for something to satisfy your darker tastes...<br></span>
  <a data-text-id="6022651401117250060" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_1742053029" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1742053029" />
    <a title="Megan✦❋Steamy Reads Blog❋✦" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/25781525-megan-steamy-reads-blog"><img alt="Megan✦❋Steamy Reads Blog❋✦" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1514899021p2/25781525.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1742053029?book_show_action=true">Aug 29, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Megan✦❋Steamy Reads Blog❋✦" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Megan✦❋Steamy Reads Blog❋✦" href="/user/show/25781525-megan-steamy-reads-blog">Megan✦❋Steamy Reads Blog❋✦</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/25781525-megan-steamy-reads-blog?shelf=abuse">abuse</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/25781525-megan-steamy-reads-blog?shelf=beautifully-written">beautifully-written</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/25781525-megan-steamy-reads-blog?shelf=emotional">emotional</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/25781525-megan-steamy-reads-blog?shelf=dark-romance">dark-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/25781525-megan-steamy-reads-blog?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/25781525-megan-steamy-reads-blog?shelf=messed-up">messed-up</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/25781525-megan-steamy-reads-blog?shelf=tortured_hero">tortured_hero</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/25781525-megan-steamy-reads-blog?shelf=dual-pov">dual-pov</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/25781525-megan-steamy-reads-blog?shelf=beautiful_broken_people">beautiful_broken_people</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/25781525-megan-steamy-reads-blog?shelf=fighter">fighter</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1742053029" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4011628654545977829"><br/><b>Warning: this book contains graphic and confronting themes which may disturb some readers. Recommended for 18+ only.</b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1472742255i/20236311._SX540_.jpg' width='450' height='400' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>
  <i>“They were always meant to be together, one boy and one girl, two hearts split into two, sent to far-off lands on their own. For God wanted to see if true love could be tested. He wanted to see if two halves of one soul could find each other again, even against the odds."</i>
</b><br/><br/>Wow! What a story. Tillie Cole really knows how to deliver a dark and twisted romance. I am absolutely in aw</span>
  <span id="freeText4011628654545977829" style="display:none"><br><b>Warning: this book contains graphic and confronting themes which may disturb some readers. Recommended for 18+ only.</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1472742255i/20236311._SX540_.jpg" width="450" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>
  <i>“They were always meant to be together, one boy and one girl, two hearts split into two, sent to far-off lands on their own. For God wanted to see if true love could be tested. He wanted to see if two halves of one soul could find each other again, even against the odds."</i>
</b><br><br>Wow! What a story. Tillie Cole really knows how to deliver a dark and twisted romance. I am absolutely in awe of Tillie Cole’s talent. She is such a versatile author. None of the books I have read by her have been the same. She has the ability to draw her readers in with her in-depth research and knowledge, captivating story lines and beautiful writing. <br><br>Imagine you had no recollection of your childhood, imagine you were only known as a number, imagine you were someone who was trained not just to fight but to kill. Prisoner 818 was taken from his family and the life he knew and was forced to endure unspeakable acts at such a young age. All he is sure of, is his need for revenge; revenge against Alik. He’s unsure as to why he needs to seek revenge against Alik, but he knows Alik is the one responsible for taking away his freedom. <br> <br><b>
  <i>“Revenge. Kill. Revenge. Maim. Alik Durov. Brooklyn, New York. Kill.”</i>
</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1472742350i/20236321._SX540_.jpg" width="450" height="450" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Kisa is living inside her own prison. As the daughter of the head of the Russian underground fighting ring known as “The Dungeon,” she has someone watching her at all times. Her whole life is planned out for her from who she’s going to marry to where she goes and to who she is allowed to talk to. Her only sanctuary, where she feels any remnant of freedom, is within her church. Little did she know that whilst volunteering to feed the homeless, she would stumble across a homeless man who would forever change her life.<br><br><b>
  <i>“I owed my life to a mysterious homeless man on the street. A homeless man who fought like a killer.”</i>
</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1472901863i/20348470._SX540_.jpg" width="400" height="350" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>I’m not going to go into the ins and outs of the story as I feel it is one you need to experience yourself, but I most definitely recommend that you read it if you enjoy dark, intense, suspenseful and compelling stories. I understand this may not be everybody’s cup of tea, as it can at times be quite disturbing; hence why there is a warning. Having said that, this is such a riveting story which had me mesmerised and intrigued from page one, right through to the last page. Hats off to Tillie Cole for writing such an intriguing, twisted yet beautiful love story. <br><br><br><br><br><br></span>

<div id="review_1144111795" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1144111795" />
    <a title="Catarina" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/11538033-catarina"><img alt="Catarina" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1514808293p2/11538033.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1144111795?book_show_action=true">Dec 28, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Catarina" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Catarina" href="/user/show/11538033-catarina">Catarina</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/24183939-raze">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11538033-catarina?shelf=i-must-like-mind-torture">i-must-like-mind-torture</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11538033-catarina?shelf=the-bad-boy-look">the-bad-boy-look</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11538033-catarina?shelf=is-getting-hot-in-here">is-getting-hot-in-here</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11538033-catarina?shelf=fighters-and-bad-asses">fighters-and-bad-asses</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11538033-catarina?shelf=oh-the-angst">oh-the-angst</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11538033-catarina?shelf=the-alpha-syndrome">the-alpha-syndrome</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1144111795" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7262620843256613728"><b>4 Home Stars</b>	<br/><br/>Raze was a boy, turned into prisoner and then turned into a human killing machine. <br/>Kisa is the daughter of a Russian mob king stuck into an engagement she never wanted. <br/>Their lives weren’t supposed to cross… but when they do, their worlds clash and suddenly they feel things for each other they shouldn’t feel. Neither of them can stop it. <br/>But when you live in a world of gangster and killers, love has no place in it. And the more you fight for it, the more you stand to lose. Not only </span>
  <span id="freeText7262620843256613728" style="display:none"><b>4 Home Stars</b>	<br><br>Raze was a boy, turned into prisoner and then turned into a human killing machine. <br>Kisa is the daughter of a Russian mob king stuck into an engagement she never wanted. <br>Their lives weren’t supposed to cross… but when they do, their worlds clash and suddenly they feel things for each other they shouldn’t feel. Neither of them can stop it. <br>But when you live in a world of gangster and killers, love has no place in it. And the more you fight for it, the more you stand to lose. Not only the person you love, but also your own life. <br><br> <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1420144177i/13180430.jpg" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>This book is not a walk on the park. It will make you feel, will make you cry, and will take on an emotional journey that you’ll not easily forget… but is sometimes so gruesome that will actually feel your gut wrenching. I’m not usually a frequent reader of this type of unconventional love stories, but I figured that if I will enter the mind-f*ck train, at least is good to have Tillie Cole as my driver. She is an amazing writer and believe me, she pulled this off. So if you’re not afraid of a little reading torture and heart aching romances, give this book a try. You will not regret. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1402872274i/10002999.jpg" width="350" height="170" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br> <b>Rating: </b> 4 Stars. <br> <b>Characters Development: </b> Raze and Kisa are amazing together. Both broken and both stuck to a life they didn’t ask for, it’s amazing to see them falling for each other, even knowing that they shouldn’t. A complex couple that we can’t help but falling for and hoping for their happily ever after. <br> <b>Steam: </b> Hot. <br> <b>Sensible Subjects: </b> <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Abuse. Rape. Kidnapping.  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br> <b>Love Triangle: </b> <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Not really. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><b>Cheating: </b> <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[No. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br> <b>HEA: </b>	<a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Yes. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

<div id="review_1138215497" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1138215497" />
    <a title="Allison ❤️Will Never Conquer Her TBR❤️" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/9080319-allison-will-never-conquer-her-tbr"><img alt="Allison ❤️Will Never Conquer Her TBR❤️" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1465384674p2/9080319.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1138215497?book_show_action=true">Dec 22, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Allison ❤️Will Never Conquer Her TBR❤️" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Allison ❤️Will Never Conquer Her TBR❤️" href="/user/show/9080319-allison-will-never-conquer-her-tbr">Allison ❤️Will Never Conquer Her TBR❤️</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9080319-allison-will-never-conquer-her-tbr?shelf=best-of-2015">best-of-2015</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1138215497" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6678821641654787808"><br/><b>4.75 Revenge-is-oh-so-sweet Stars!<br/><br/><br/><a href='http://s1320.photobucket.com/user/allipalk/media/Mobile%20Uploads/2015-01/30901B0C-B5AB-479B-BCFA-CF7F5BA55C0E_zpsp9dsximh.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1420250841i/13197951._SY540_.jpg' alt=' photo 30901B0C-B5AB-479B-BCFA-CF7F5BA55C0E_zpsp9dsximh.jpg' width='400' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/></a><br/><br/><br/><i>“They were always meant to be together, one boy and one girl, two hearts split into two, sent to far-off lands on their own. For God wanted to see if true love could be tested. He wanted to see if two halves of one soul could find each other again, even against the odds. Years would pass, they would both be hurt, they would both be sad, but one day, when they least expected it, they would stumble into each other’s paths. The question is: would they recognize eac</i></b></span>
  <span id="freeText6678821641654787808" style="display:none"><br><b>4.75 Revenge-is-oh-so-sweet Stars!<br><br><br><a href="http://s1320.photobucket.com/user/allipalk/media/Mobile%20Uploads/2015-01/30901B0C-B5AB-479B-BCFA-CF7F5BA55C0E_zpsp9dsximh.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1420250841i/13197951._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo 30901B0C-B5AB-479B-BCFA-CF7F5BA55C0E_zpsp9dsximh.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a><br><br><br><i>“They were always meant to be together, one boy and one girl, two hearts split into two, sent to far-off lands on their own. For God wanted to see if true love could be tested. He wanted to see if two halves of one soul could find each other again, even against the odds. Years would pass, they would both be hurt, they would both be sad, but one day, when they least expected it, they would stumble into each other’s paths. The question is: would they recognize each other’s soul? Would they find their way back to love…?”</i></b><br><br><br><br>The above fairy tale synopsis is the heart of the book. It's a long quote, I know, but I loved how the author took such a dark, gritty plot and, deep down, made it what fairy tales are made of in the end. But, rest assured, this ain't no heart and flowers Cinderella story. <br><br><br>Anywho, <b>Raze</b> was an intense story of a man, taken as a teenager, brainwashed and tortured, fed with drugs and steroids to forget everything he once was and morf him into a death-seeking cage fighter. He's no longer Luka. He's simply 818, one of the most feared, undefeated killers in the underground fighting ring. "Raze" knows nothing of his past self...nothing except a few words on his cell wall...a name, a location, <i>revenge!</i><br><br><br><br><a href="http://s1320.photobucket.com/user/allipalk/media/Mobile%20Uploads/2015-01/F664519F-573C-45FE-980F-E09AC7449600_zpssb2lvpiy.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1420251411i/13197999._SX540_.jpg" alt=" photo F664519F-573C-45FE-980F-E09AC7449600_zpssb2lvpiy.jpg" width="400" height="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br><br>Kisa Volkova, daughter of a Russian mafia lord, is betrothed to a monster, Alik Durov...son of the second in line mafia lord. Her life is arranged, and while not being in love with Alik (in fact, hating him), she plays the role of dutiful mafia princess and future wife. <br><br><br>Until one fateful night when a stranger saves her life. Delivering care packages to the homeless in New York City, she's attacked. Suddenly, from the shadows, she's saved by a hooded man. A man who bears a striking resemblance to her long lost best friend, first love, and soul mate. He hides his eyes behind the hood but there's something about him...<a href="http://s1320.photobucket.com/user/allipalk/media/scroll%20Art/1D494C1E-55CF-4F8A-81D7-4C22B1E6890A_zpscuekowdg.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1420297227i/13201348.jpg" alt=" photo 1D494C1E-55CF-4F8A-81D7-4C22B1E6890A_zpscuekowdg.jpg" width="400" height="200" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br>Raze didn't disappoint me in providing an intense, dark, gritty, yet angsty love story. It had all the elements of a read that I crave. My heart was racing, the build-up perfectly timed, the characters believable. It wasn't hearts and flowers but in a sense, it was to me. It was such an awesome angsty love story. A story of second chances. <br><br><br><b>
  <i>“Whatever our souls are made of, his and mine are the same."</i>
</b><br><a href="http://s1320.photobucket.com/user/allipalk/media/scroll%20Art/1D494C1E-55CF-4F8A-81D7-4C22B1E6890A_zpscuekowdg.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1420297227i/13201348.jpg" alt=" photo 1D494C1E-55CF-4F8A-81D7-4C22B1E6890A_zpscuekowdg.jpg" width="400" height="200" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a>My heart broke for both Kisa and Raze (aka Luka). She's engaged to a monster yet accepts her fate because it's the mafia way. She fears Alik but takes his sadistic violent side knowing she was born into this life. Luka...where to begin. He's a shell of what he was when he was taken as a teen. Seeing Kisa being attacked stirred something from within to protect this stranger but that's all he can take from it. He doesn't recall anything except...<br><br> <i>Alik Durov<br>Brooklyn, New York<br>Revenge<br>Kill </i><br><br><br>The only reason I deducted a minuscule .25 star is because it all kind of wraps up a bit too easily and a couple parts were (a bit) cheesy. But that's seriously just me being picky. I love a book that captures me the way this book did. Providing me with all the elements of a story I devour. Tillie Cole is quickly turning into an auto-buy for me. Not everyone can do dark. She pulls it off superbly!! I highly recommend this book to readers that crave more than just angsty romance. Throw in the mafia, a fair amount of violence, suspense, darkness, revenge, steam and it's literary perfection!<br><br>And I thank you!<br><br><a href="http://s1320.photobucket.com/user/allipalk/media/Blowing%20Kisses/90BEAF62-BBB5-4905-9A58-C8E6B4700766_zpsquw4ikav.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1408487855ra/10855964.gif" alt=" photo 90BEAF62-BBB5-4905-9A58-C8E6B4700766_zpsquw4ikav.gif" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a></span>
  <a data-text-id="6678821641654787808" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_1062252958" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1062252958" />
    <a title="Christie«SHBBblogger»" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/6650940-christie-shbbblogger"><img alt="Christie«SHBBblogger»" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1537729030p2/6650940.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1062252958?book_show_action=true">Sep 23, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Christie«SHBBblogger»" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Christie«SHBBblogger»" href="/user/show/6650940-christie-shbbblogger">Christie«SHBBblogger»</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6650940-christie-shbbblogger?shelf=big-girl-panties-read">big-girl-panties-read</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6650940-christie-shbbblogger?shelf=abused-in-childhood">abused-in-childhood</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6650940-christie-shbbblogger?shelf=reunited-and-it-feels-so-good">reunited-and-it-feels-so-good</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6650940-christie-shbbblogger?shelf=unputdownable">unputdownable</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6650940-christie-shbbblogger?shelf=alpha-hero">alpha-hero</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6650940-christie-shbbblogger?shelf=why-didnt-i-read-this-earlier">why-didnt-i-read-this-earlier</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6650940-christie-shbbblogger?shelf=tortured-hero">tortured-hero</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6650940-christie-shbbblogger?shelf=has-a-playlist">has-a-playlist</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6650940-christie-shbbblogger?shelf=boxer-fighter-mma">boxer-fighter-mma</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6650940-christie-shbbblogger?shelf=heroine-with-a-stalker-killer">heroine-with-a-stalker-killer</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1062252958" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15311855925143271179"><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1489274209i/22201529.jpg' width='400' height='40' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>Title:</b>Raze<br/><b>Series:</b>Scarred Souls #1<br/><b>Author:</b>Tillie Cole<br/><b>Release date: </b>December 30, 2014<br/><b>Rating:</b>5 stars<br/><b>Cliffhanger:</b>No<br/><b> HEA: </b> <a class='jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction'>(view spoiler)</a><span class='spoilerContainer' style='display: none'>[Yes  <a class='jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction'>(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1420471499i/13229692._SY540_.jpg' width='400' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>This book is essentially about the depths of depravity and torment that one man must endure to make his way to freedom and the one woman who was born to be his. Luka Tolstoi is one of three princes of New York's Russian Mafiya. Kisa Volkova is the Mafiya princess who had his heart from the first time he set eyes on her as a child. And those eyes.</span>
  <span id="freeText15311855925143271179" style="display:none"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1489274209i/22201529.jpg" width="400" height="40" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Title:</b>Raze<br><b>Series:</b>Scarred Souls #1<br><b>Author:</b>Tillie Cole<br><b>Release date: </b>December 30, 2014<br><b>Rating:</b>5 stars<br><b>Cliffhanger:</b>No<br><b> HEA: </b> <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Yes  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1420471499i/13229692._SY540_.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>This book is essentially about the depths of depravity and torment that one man must endure to make his way to freedom and the one woman who was born to be his. Luka Tolstoi is one of three princes of New York's Russian Mafiya. Kisa Volkova is the Mafiya princess who had his heart from the first time he set eyes on her as a child. And those eyes. *sigh* I loved the detail about his eyes holding a piece of hers inside them-it was such a romantic piece of an otherwise violent and brutal story. <br><br><b>Mama said God placed a piece of my eye within his so we would always know we shared one soul.</b><br><br>If it weren't for things like this, I don't know if I would have loved the book as much, although as beautifully as it was written I know I still would have appreciated its impact on me. This book is one that will hopefully reach inside you and make you hurt for this horribly wronged and tortured hero. I know I did. But what this man becomes in order to keep his body and soul intact makes his fated love story all the more powerful and significant. What he becomes is a monster, a killer.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1420477317i/13230208._SY540_.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>In these three families, there is a betrayal, a murder, and an injustice. Luka is sent away and he's lost forever, even to himself. He's sent to Hell on earth-a place where boys go and fight to the death, they're tortured, beaten, and treated as animals. Only the strongest of the strong survive for long and Luka (now Raze) becomes a stone cold killing machine with no thoughts other than training and his next kill. Until his escape. Now he has one thought, one goal:<br><br><b>Revenge.</b><br><br>Kisa is the dutiful Mafiya daughter. She loves her family, and though she's terrified of her fiancé, Alik Durov, she continues to do whatever is required of her and take his abuse. After Luka is sent away, she became almost numb and he was able to slip in and take control of her. Alik is an extremely dangerous and abusive person, but Kisa blindly ignores the signs that he could easily eventually kill her. One one hand, it was really frustrating how she allows his horrible treatment of her. He was really scary with her and she never speaks up and talks to her family about it. But the way she mentally checked out after losing her soul mate makes it believable, though I didn't like it. <br><br><b>I hardly recognized the girl before me anymore. She got lost somewhere over the years, hiding away, running for her life.</b><br><br>Raze returns to New York and when he and Kisa's paths intersect again, he feels that same immediate urge to protect her even though he holds no memories of his past. Everything before the underground prison is a total blank. (You're probably wondering how he remembers who to get revenge on if he has no memory, but that is explained with a rational explanation.) Tortured out of him through electric shock and drugs. But being near her starts making him <i>feel</i> things. <br><br><b>Warmth filled my chest like the sun had moved its home inside of me. I'd only ever felt cold before. The cell was cold. Killing was cold...I was always cold, but right now, I was warm...I felt alive. No longer dead inside.</b><br><br> Kisa is just as conflicted. This man who appears to be the love of her life, who she believed was dead isn't the same man she holds in her memories. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1420479248i/13230576._SY540_.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>This couple is anything but your average sweethearts. What they both have to endure is downright gutting at times. So much pain, heartbreak, and injustice. I wanted an emotional read that would really hit hard and that's what I found in Raze. Tillie Cole leaves me breathless how she can depict each scene with such skill that every one of my senses are right there inside the world she creates. Feeling, seeing, and hearing every emotion and experience that each character experiences. This was one of those books for me that I started late at night and literally was so transported into the story that I fell asleep while holding my kindle, woke up, and immediately read the last section of the book. It's the definition of un-put-downable for me. Would I recommend this book? Hell yes, I would. I was nervous to try this one out because I thought it might be too difficult to read but that wasn't the case at all. It's well worth the pain for the beauty of Kisa and Luka.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1420480208i/13230652._SY540_.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>FOLLOW SMOKIN HOT BOOK BLOG ON: <b><br><br><a href="https://twitter.com/BlogSmokin/" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener"><img alt="Twitter" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1391768351i/8452934.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a><a href="http://facebook.com/smokinhotbookblog" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener"><img alt="Facebook" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1391768485i/8452963.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a><a And the plot line was just PERFECT! Because of how the ending turned out, it was totally worth it trudging through all the disturbing scenes in this book :D</span>

              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1181801129343759711">Find all of my reviews at: <a target='_blank' rel='noopener nofollow' href='http://52bookminimum.blogspot.com/'>http://52bookminimum.blogspot.com/</a><br/><br/>This review is brought to you by . . . <br/><br/><a href='http://www.freeimagehosting.net/commercial-photography/' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1423966458i/13695832._SY540_.jpg' alt='Commercial Photography' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/>(Now in convenient travel sizes!)<br/><br/><b>RELEASE THE KRAKEN!!!!</b><br/><br/>As some of you know I've been doing my local library's Winter Reading Challenge in order to score a new coffee mug. My satisfaction with the recommended selections of said challenge has been less than stellar. To top it off, on Thursday I discovered that my reward for completing the challenge this year wouldn't even be a coffee mug. Instea</span>
  <span id="freeText1181801129343759711" style="display:none">Find all of my reviews at: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://52bookminimum.blogspot.com/">http://52bookminimum.blogspot.com/</a><br><br>This review is brought to you by . . . <br><br><a href="http://www.freeimagehosting.net/commercial-photography/" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1423966458i/13695832._SY540_.jpg" alt="Commercial Photography" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br>(Now in convenient travel sizes!)<br><br><b>RELEASE THE KRAKEN!!!!</b><br><br>As some of you know I've been doing my local library's Winter Reading Challenge in order to score a new coffee mug. My satisfaction with the recommended selections of said challenge has been less than stellar. To top it off, on Thursday I discovered that my reward for completing the challenge this year wouldn't even be a coffee mug. Instead it would be a cocktail glass. I was already tired of waiting for my final "romance" selection to queue up, so I opted to read some porn in order to turn in my paperwork early and get the f-ing stupid glass . . . and so the drunken review of <i>Raze</i> was born. Bottoms up!<br><br><a href="http://www.freeimagehosting.net/commercial-photography/" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1423966458i/13695833._SY540_.jpg" alt="Commercial Photography" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Quick question before I get started. How many of you have ever referred to the lady garden as the "channel"??????<br><br><a href="http://www.freeimagehosting.net/commercial-photography/" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1423966458ra/13695834.gif" alt="Commercial Photography" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Right. That's what I thought. We'll get back to that a bit later. Now on with the review!<br><br>Here's the problem. If I were rating the plot, this one would get a solid 3.5 Star rating. The premise is this dude has spent half his life in the Gulag - he has been drugged, brainwashed, and forced to fight to the death in an underground fighting ring in order to survive . . . <br><br><a href="http://www.freeimagehosting.net/commercial-photography/" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1423966458ra/13695835.gif" alt="Commercial Photography" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Oh right, my apologies. Anyway, "that of which I shall not speak" was good. Super brutal and the action was intense. It might've even been good enough to score a 4 Star if the prisoner weren't known as "818." Now, I'm sure I'm in the minority with this weird knowledge, but anytime 3-digit numbers are referenced I think of zip codes, and this particular zip code is for The Valley . . . <br><br><a href="http://www.freeimagehosting.net/commercial-photography/" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1423966458ra/13695836.gif" alt="Commercial Photography" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Random, but those are the things that stick in my pop-culture addled brain.<br><br>Long story even longer, Prisoner 818 has one goal in life - to seek revenge on a man he remembers nothing about, except for his name. Whilst seeking revenge 818 (a/k/a "Raze") finds himself joining another fighting ring (known as "The Dungeon"), but this time it's led by the Russian Bratva. As he sets his sights on revenge, Raze finds his eye also drawn to Kisa, the woman who helps run The Dungeon. <br><br>I'm sure you can figure out what happens next. You guessed it, it's time for some bow-chicka-wow-wow. Unfortunately, one of my friends just decided to leave Goodreads, but I think he said it best when he said the cover looked like a "tiger in a hoodie." Yep. And I wanted to bang that tiger. What I didn't know was that the parts of the book discussing the naughty business would make me feel a little something like this . . . <br><br><a href="http://www.freeimagehosting.net/commercial-photography/" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1423966458ra/13695837.gif" alt="Commercial Photography" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>And that I would learn everything I never wanted to know about Kisa's "channel" . . . <br><br><a href="http://www.freeimagehosting.net/commercial-photography/" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1423966697ra/13695873.gif" alt="Commercial Photography" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Right? I mean CHANNEL?!?!?!?!?! Maybe it's just me, but doesn't your brain conjure up something wide and <i>vast</i> when you hear "channel"????? Something kind of like . . . <br><br><a href="http://www.freeimagehosting.net/commercial-photography/" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1423966458ra/13695839.gif" alt="Commercial Photography" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>If you want to have a lot of fun while reading this one, take a drink every time anyone talks about the "channel" . . . <br><br><a href="http://www.freeimagehosting.net/commercial-photography/" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1423966458ra/13695840.gif" alt="Commercial Photography" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>But whatever you do, don't add any other icky words to the game. Drinking during "channel" talk might result in something like this . . .<br><br><a href="http://www.freeimagehosting.net/commercial-photography/" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1423966807ra/13695883.gif" alt="Commercial Photography" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>But if you add in references to Kisa's lady bits being called . . . <br><br><a href="http://www.freeimagehosting.net/commercial-photography/" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1423966458ra/13695842.gif" alt="Commercial Photography" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><a href="http://www.freeimagehosting.net/commercial-photography/" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1423966458ra/13695843.gif" alt="Commercial Photography" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br>(Spock <b>does not</b> approve of such pussy talk!)<br><br><b>Sidenote</b>: Someone asked me to work that Spock .gif into a review a long time ago. NAILED IT!<br><br>Where was I? Oh yeah, don't add any pussy speak to the drinking game or else you might find yourself in Pam Poovey territory . . . <br><br><a href="http://www.freeimagehosting.net/commercial-photography/" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1423966458ra/13695844.gif" alt="Commercial Photography" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Speaking of Pam Poovey, I think Kisa must have taken some notes on how to have a "successful" sexytime from my pal. If references to . . . ummmmm . . . <i>moisture</i> squick you out, bring a barf bag . . . <br><br><a href="http://www.freeimagehosting.net/commercial-photography/" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1423966458ra/13695845.gif" alt="Commercial Photography" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Recommended to those who have a <b>lot</b> more experience with dirty books than lil' ol' me.</span>

    <a title="Jen" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/6049062-jen"><img alt="Jen" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1460575899p2/6049062.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1148078298?book_show_action=true">Dec 31, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jen" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jen" href="/user/show/6049062-jen">Jen</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1148078298" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11811879160161860803">What a wonderful way to end/start the new year! OMG!! I LOVE RAZE!!! What have I been reading?? "I am in a RAZE HAZE!!!" I have seen that quote around Facebook, and that is exactly how I am feeling at the moment! This book checked off all of my boxes that make me fall in love with a hero. Raze was a tortured individual who endured far more than anyone should ever have to; but when he lays his eyes on Kisa it is like his heart starts beating for the first time. Yes, some may say this book comes a</span>
  <span id="freeText11811879160161860803" style="display:none">What a wonderful way to end/start the new year! OMG!! I LOVE RAZE!!! What have I been reading?? "I am in a RAZE HAZE!!!" I have seen that quote around Facebook, and that is exactly how I am feeling at the moment! This book checked off all of my boxes that make me fall in love with a hero. Raze was a tortured individual who endured far more than anyone should ever have to; but when he lays his eyes on Kisa it is like his heart starts beating for the first time. Yes, some may say this book comes across as a tad corny...but not me! For me, it was romance at its finest. It is raw,gritty, and at times brutal,gory and gruesome; but the moments that Kisa and Raze are together...my pulse was pounding and I was breathless! The intensity of this couple will be hard to be in stories to come. I should have expected this was going to be an epic read for me, as Tillie Cole is a newly discovered author for me and I love anything she writes! I would literally read the phone book if she wrote it! Her books are on the darker side; but wow, when her characters fall in love...they do it with their whole souls! To me, that is what a romance book should be about!<br /><br />In "Raze" we are shown a very dark side of life where there are kids groomed to be fighters. Not just fighters though, they need to fight to the death. Basically, they become stone cold killers. Raze is no exception. He was taken from his old life and tortured and conditioned to forget who he was or where he came from. Instead, his life became about survival, countless torture, and living in a cell. Eventually, Raze lost his humanity and lived on instinct alone.<br /><br />The heroine; Kisa Volkova, lives in her own kind of jail. Her father is the head of the Russian underground (the New York Russian Bratva)her life has been dictated for her and she is engaged to a horrible man by the name of Alik Durov. Alik is a pshycotic a-hole, and that is an understatement; believe me! He gives new meaning to the word controlling and possessive..and let's face it...downright nasty! There is history between Kisa and Alik going all of the way back to when they were children. Kisa feels she has no choice but to marry him, as it is what is expected of her. That is, until the day that she lays eyes on a man name Raze. Then....all bets are off, and the real story begins!!!! Take my word for it....this is a story you don't want to miss!<br /><br />I could go on all day gushing about this book; but all I can say is that I highly recommend it! The writing is superb, the sex is beyond passionate, primal, and majorly intense. This will be going on my absolute favorite for 2015!! Hooray! What an awesome way to bring in the New Year! Thank you Tillie Cole for writing another masterpiece!!!!</span>
  <a data-text-id="11811879160161860803" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

  <span id="freeText18413683270087627376" style="display:none"><strong>Book</strong> – Raze<br> <strong>Author</strong> – Tillie Cole<br><strong>Publication Date</strong> – December 30, 2014<br> <strong>Genre</strong> –Dark Romance<br> <strong>Type</strong> – Stand Alone <br> <strong>Cliffhanger</strong> – No<br> <strong>Rating</strong> – 4 out of 5 Stars<br> <br> <em>Own a copy.</em><br><em> </em><br><br> <strong>My Thoughts - Story</strong><br> If you had to ask me one word to describe this book, it would be:<br><br><strong>ADDICTIVE</strong><br><br>Once I picked it up and got through the first 50 or so pages, I was hooked…(line and sinker).  Yes, there were a few things I found a bit “over the top” but shit…we are reading about fantasies here…not what is going on outside our front door. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1420315141i/13203404._SX540_.jpg" alt="" width="540" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>There are a few books that can draw me into the story where I can relate to the characters and yearn to be there right along with them. This was one of those special books to me.  I cried for Raze….I sympathized with Kisa and wanted to kill Alik.<br><br>This author is very descriptive with her writing and brings you into the story where every little detail is explained to a point where you feel like a movie is playing out in your head.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1420315141i/13203405._SY540_.jpg" alt="" width="500" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>My final words on this is that I am so happy Bev talked me into reading this!!<br><br><strong>Re-Cap</strong><br> Damn…I hate this part of the review because I am always fearful that I will give too much away and ruin the story for you. So, I’ll try to stay as general as possible…<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1420315141i/13203406._SX540_.jpg" alt="" width="540" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Kisa is the Russian princess of the NY underground. She heads up the death match and is engaged to Alik (the prince and heir). One day while atoning for her family’s sins with the church, she gets attacked and a mysterious stranger saves her life.  Instantly, Kisa feels a pull with this strange giant and can’t help herself from searching him out.  He only has 1 thing on his mind though, REVENGE. Revenge against the man who put him in a Russian jail that turned him into the monster he now is.  Revenge against Alik.<br><br>I’ll leave you there…that consists of the first 50 pages and will get you started to find out what happens between Raze, Alik and Lisa.  How the past may come back to haunt all of those involved.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1420315141i/13203407._SY540_.jpg" alt="" width="440" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><strong>Reason for Reading –</strong><strong> </strong>Recommended by Bev<br> <strong>Story –</strong><strong> </strong>5 out of 5 Stars<br> <strong>Steam –</strong><strong> </strong> 4 out of 5 Stars<br> <strong>Angst –</strong><strong> </strong>4 out of 5 Stars<br> <strong>Writing –</strong><strong> </strong>3.5 out of 5 Stars<br> <strong>Content Flow –</strong><strong> </strong>4 out of 5 Stars<br><strong>Told In</strong> – Dual POV<br><strong>Heroine/Personality –</strong><strong> </strong>Kisa…I loved her character and felt she was such a strong influence<br><strong>Hero/Personality –</strong><strong> </strong>Raze…I found myself loving his character and empathy for the life he missed.<br><strong>HEA (Spoiler) - </strong><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Yes <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><strong>Would Read More from Author?</strong><strong> </strong>Yes<br> <strong>Recommend To –</strong><strong> </strong>Anyone who doesn’t mind a bit of darkness tied in with their romance.  <br><br><strong>For more Reviews, Free E-books and Giveaways</strong><br><div>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1137056116" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11965007628658016304"><b>4.5 Solnyshko STARS</b><br/><br/>This is a story written with a lot of heart and soul. It’s dark, raw, gritty and dangerous but also filled with heart-crushing love. Go in with an open mind and your world will be rocked.<br/><br/><a href='http://imgur.com/e3ihdkv' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1420262953ra/13199101.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/><b>
  <i>“They were always meant to be together, one boy and one girl, two hearts split into two, sent to far-off lands on their own. For God wanted to see if true love could be tested. He wanted to see if two halves of one soul could find each other again, even against the odds.”</i>
</b><br/><br/><a href='http://imgur.com/uNT4lqA' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1420263300ra/13199118.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/><b>A boy. A g</b></span>
  <span id="freeText11965007628658016304" style="display:none"><b>4.5 Solnyshko STARS</b><br><br>This is a story written with a lot of heart and soul. It’s dark, raw, gritty and dangerous but also filled with heart-crushing love. Go in with an open mind and your world will be rocked.<br><br><a href="http://imgur.com/e3ihdkv" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1420262953ra/13199101.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>
  <i>“They were always meant to be together, one boy and one girl, two hearts split into two, sent to far-off lands on their own. For God wanted to see if true love could be tested. He wanted to see if two halves of one soul could find each other again, even against the odds.”</i>
</b><br><br><a href="http://imgur.com/uNT4lqA" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1420263300ra/13199118.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>A boy. A girl. The beach. <i>“Can I have you?”</i></b><br><a href="http://s1292.photobucket.com/user/swidso/media/e6efb229c1a0205adb2841c5ab009546_zpsda1f2b77.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1420262953i/13199103._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo e6efb229c1a0205adb2841c5ab009546_zpsda1f2b77.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>“Three boys. Three boys by the falls. On a family vacation. Two of them best friends. The third had a knife.”<br><a href="http://s1292.photobucket.com/user/swidso/media/37508997_zpsbcab1773.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1420262953i/13199104._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo 37508997_zpsbcab1773.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a><br><br>Death. A killer. No memory and one focus – revenge. Rough, raw, dark, dangerous, intimidating. <br><a href="http://s1292.photobucket.com/user/swidso/media/Raze_zps533c8220.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1420262953i/13199105._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo Raze_zps533c8220.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a><br><br>A Russian Mafyia Princess. Abused. Prisoner. Lost and Alone.<br><a href="http://s1292.photobucket.com/user/swidso/media/Kisa_zpsedb3a549.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1420262953i/13199106._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo Kisa_zpsedb3a549.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a><br><br>“Why do I feel like I’ve known you all my life?”<br><a href="http://s1292.photobucket.com/user/swidso/media/05db517d7d4e0acc544d4e0634077403_zps1a1ec6df.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1420262954i/13199107._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo 05db517d7d4e0acc544d4e0634077403_zps1a1ec6df.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a><br><br><br>“Whatever our souls are made of—"<br>“His and mine are the same...”<br><br><a href="http://imgur.com/YDH55NM" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1410580340ra/11126778.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a><br><br>"You can have me, solnyshko. You can have all of me. You always have, and you always will."</b><br><br>I only recently discovered Ms. Cole with my read of <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/22020052.It_Ain_t_Me__Babe__Hades_Hangmen___1_" title="It Ain't Me, Babe (Hades Hangmen, #1) by Tillie Cole" rel="nofollow noopener">It Ain't Me, Babe</a> and I've become a Fan! So far, every book I've read from her has left a mark and brought a wide range of emotions and enjoyment. Raze is among these great reads!</span>
  <a data-text-id="11965007628658016304" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>
