  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1144122850" />
    <a title="Sandy ღCoffee Addict Booksღ" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/28806659-sandy-coffee-addict-books"><img alt="Sandy ღCoffee Addict Booksღ" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1437129491p2/28806659.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1144122850?book_show_action=true">Dec 28, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Sandy ღCoffee Addict Booksღ" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Sandy ღCoffee Addict Booksღ" href="/user/show/28806659-sandy-coffee-addict-books">Sandy ღCoffee Addict Booksღ</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/24183939-raze">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/28806659-sandy-coffee-addict-books?shelf=alpha-hero">alpha-hero</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/28806659-sandy-coffee-addict-books?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/28806659-sandy-coffee-addict-books?shelf=book-boyfriends">book-boyfriends</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/28806659-sandy-coffee-addict-books?shelf=cry-baby">cry-baby</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/28806659-sandy-coffee-addict-books?shelf=suspense-mystery">suspense-mystery</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/28806659-sandy-coffee-addict-books?shelf=swoon-worthy">swoon-worthy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/28806659-sandy-coffee-addict-books?shelf=hotness-alert">hotness-alert</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/28806659-sandy-coffee-addict-books?shelf=emotional">emotional</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/28806659-sandy-coffee-addict-books?shelf=favorite-couple">favorite-couple</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/28806659-sandy-coffee-addict-books?shelf=ooo-a-bad-boy">ooo-a-bad-boy</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1144122850" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2255504902953594382"><br/><b>“4.25 <i> Sand. Sun and the Sea</i>…stars”</b> <br/><br/>There are plenty of adjectives I could use to describe this book, but right now all I can think about is<br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1433950618ra/15160736.gif' width='380' height='220' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/> <br/><br/><b>And yet again Tillie Cole blew me away with her consuming storyline, intense characters and passionate love story.</b><blockquote>
  <i>“They were always meant to be together, one boy and one girl, two hearts split into two, sent to far-off lands on their own. For God wanted to see if true love could be tested. He wanted to see if two halves of one soul could find each other </i></blockquote></span>
  <span id="freeText2255504902953594382" style="display:none"><br><b>“4.25 <i> Sand. Sun and the Sea</i>…stars”</b> <br><br>There are plenty of adjectives I could use to describe this book, but right now all I can think about is<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1433950618ra/15160736.gif" width="380" height="220" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br><b>And yet again Tillie Cole blew me away with her consuming storyline, intense characters and passionate love story.</b><blockquote>
  <i>“They were always meant to be together, one boy and one girl, two hearts split into two, sent to far-off lands on their own. For God wanted to see if true love could be tested. He wanted to see if two halves of one soul could find each other again, even against the odds. Years would pass. They would both be hurt. They would both be sad, but one day, when they least expected it, they would stumble into each other’s paths. The question is: would they recognize each other’s soul? And would they find their way back to love…?”</i>
</blockquote>Well, this very first passage from the book says it all. With <b>Raze</b> aka 818 being a tormented killing machine, a monster who has no memories of his past life and <b>Kisa</b> who lost everything good in her life, a prisoner in her own shell, this is the story of <b> love loss despair and revenge.</b><br><br><b>
  <i>“Their love story began on the day she was born…”</i>
</b><br><br>Did it make my heart slam against my chest??? Hell yeah!!!! It had my utmost attention throughout, kept me on the edge for most parts, there wasn’t a single scene where I thought it was boring or flat but perfect balance of <b>darkness and innocence</b>. Tillie Cole writes dark romance with utterly damaged characters, loads of violence making it gritty and gut wrenching yet she brings out overwhelming emotion of love making your heart all gooey!!!<blockquote>
  <b>
    <i> “Whatever our souls are made of—”<br>“His and mine are the same...” </i>
  </b>
</blockquote></span>

<div id="review_2364196758" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2364196758" />
    <a title="Dilek VT" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/49572641-dilek-vt"><img alt="Dilek VT" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1448923258p2/49572641.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2364196758?book_show_action=true">Apr 17, 2018</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Dilek VT" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Dilek VT" href="/user/show/49572641-dilek-vt">Dilek VT</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/49572641-dilek-vt?shelf=soul-mates">soul-mates</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/49572641-dilek-vt?shelf=dark-and-twisted">dark-and-twisted</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/49572641-dilek-vt?shelf=murder-torture">murder-torture</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/49572641-dilek-vt?shelf=violence-trauma">violence-trauma</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/49572641-dilek-vt?shelf=rape">rape</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/49572641-dilek-vt?shelf=abuse">abuse</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/49572641-dilek-vt?shelf=mafia">mafia</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/49572641-dilek-vt?shelf=weak-heroine">weak-heroine</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/49572641-dilek-vt?shelf=illegal-activity">illegal-activity</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/49572641-dilek-vt?shelf=damaged-broken-hero">damaged-broken-hero</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2364196758" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14190295981192304821">I am not into "dark" books but I decided that a book which begins like this is worth trying...<br/><br/><i>“They were always meant to be together, one boy and one girl, two hearts split into two, sent to far-off lands on their own. For God wanted to see if true love could be tested. He wanted to see if two halves of one soul could find each other again, even against the odds. Years would pass. They would both be hurt. They would both be sad, but one day, when they least expected it, they would stumble into e</i></span>
  <span id="freeText14190295981192304821" style="display:none">I am not into "dark" books but I decided that a book which begins like this is worth trying...<br><br><i>“They were always meant to be together, one boy and one girl, two hearts split into two, sent to far-off lands on their own. For God wanted to see if true love could be tested. He wanted to see if two halves of one soul could find each other again, even against the odds. Years would pass. They would both be hurt. They would both be sad, but one day, when they least expected it, they would stumble into each other’s paths. The question is: would they recognize each other’s soul? And would they find their way back to love…?”</i><br><br>***********************************************<br><br>As you can see from the above, I thought this was going to be a book about an epic love between two soul mates but now that I have finished it, I am shell-shocked at what I have read. The romance is buried deep under the weight of all the ugliness that spreads all over the book. <br><br>What dominates the whole book is the doings of the Russian mafia, pure violence, torture, brutality, rough violent sex, abuse of children and teens, rape, murder etc.<br><br>The intended epic love story is tainted and repressed by the ugliness dominating the whole book.<br><br>***********************************************<br><br>There are so many reviews about this book telling about the plot, so I will not talk about the plot at all. It’s just enough if you know that there is Russian Mafia and their bloody life stories in it.<br><br><b>I will just tell you why I didn’t like this book.</b><br><br>1.	The soul-mates, Luka and Kisa had their first sex when she was 13 and Luka was 14 years old. <br><br>Am I the only one who thinks it is too early??? I believe it is wrong on so many levels. I am disturbed by the fact that it is romanticized!<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1481034322ra/21377041.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>And when Luka is taken from Kisa, Alik takes his place immediately and he has been having sex with her since that age (Kisa 13, Alik 14). Again, so very wrong for me.<br><br>P.S. No use of protection mentioned.<br><br>2.	Alik is a disturbed and sadistic man. Kisa is a heroine that takes submissive to a whole new level. <br><br>We witness their relationship when she is 25 years old. Every time Alik has sex with her, it is violent and brutal but she somehow accepts it the way it is and the more interesting thing was that she can have an orgasm during that brutal act. <br><br>Kisa knows Alik likes to kill people and torture them. She believes she needs to be with him because she is the one who calms him even a little bit. I wanted to puke every time she expressed this rationale of hers. <br><br>She accepted this obsessive man’s all rules. For example, she was forbidden to talk to other men, she was forbidden to go out with friends, she wasn’t allowed to go out of the house at all - period!<br><br>She was taken by bodyguards to the Gym the Bratva owned and where she worked. Then, she was brought home by the same bodyguard.<br><br>She had to wear clothes that covered all her body because Alik didn’t like anyone to look at her. He killed many just because they looked at her. <br><br>And he beats her if she talks to a man. It doesn't matter about what. She is forbidden to talk to men and she has to comply. <br><br>Those clothes that covered all her body also helped to hide the bruises Alik gave her every time she did something wrong.<br><br>I didn’t understand what kind of a mafia princess she was. She let Alik abuse her in every way possible. She knew he went to other whores as well. He explained to her that she wasn’t like them but she was special. She heard that some women he had sex with didn't survive Alik's violence and she thought she was lucky because he would never hurt her that much. <br><br>Kisa says she accepted this life with Alik because she was afraid to leave him. She also thought she had only Alik but no one else since Luka died. (All other men are wiped from the face of the Earth, it seems?!)<br><br>She even felt compassion for that scumbag. She never thought of complaining to her father about the violence of Alik towards her. He seemed to love his daughter, so I didn’t understand her rationale and acceptance of that life at all. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1524009437ra/25393873.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Oh, one more thing I hated about Kisa: In the Gym The Bratva owned and where Kisa works, there are cage fights organized. And the fights are to the death. One fighter gets out of the cage alive because the fight ends only when one fighter dies. Kisa never expresses her discomfort about what is happening in that Gym. It is her normal and she is used to this life. Even Luka (Raze) cuts himself every time he kills a person and leaves a mark on his body just to remember what he has done but I don’t remember reading any sentences where Kisa expresses her sadness about the fighters that die in that Gym, (which is in fact an illegal underground place.)<br><br>3.	Raze/Luka is a scarred soul. He is beyond damaged. My heart ached for him. He has been forced to kill more than 600 people in those 12 years. He has been beaten, raped, drugged and tortured. He has been taught to kill or the other option was to be killed. <br><br>That’s why, it was just unbelievable for me that he would be healed from all those terrible experiences just by reuniting with his long-lost love. He needed therapy – serious &amp; long sessions of therapy. <br><br>The writer tries to make us believe that he can sleep without nightmares when Kisa sleeps with him… Sorry, I am not buying that! Go live in that hell for 12 years and then, go sleep with your lover and feel Ok, and then come and talk about it that easily! Pffttt!<br><br>4.	Personally, I do not prefer my heroes &amp; heroines virgin. So if they have been with each other only, their love story is not my cuppa. <br><br>In this case, Luka has only been with Kisa. And after that one time with Luka at the age of 13, Kisa has been with Alik for so many years. So, two men for Kisa.<br><br>When Luka and Kisa find each other after so many years, Luka was a man who never had any other women in his life. And after having been raped for so many years in that dungeon by the guards, Luka forgot how to make love and he didn’t know what to do with Kisa at first when they started to sleep together. He tried to do what the guards did to him. She had to teach him how to do it. Reading those parts where she tried to teach him what to do was unbearable for me. Inexperience is something I never prefer in my heroes in books!<br><br>5.	And the last reason I didn’t like this book was because it was too depressing. It just sucked the life out of me. So much blood, violence, brutality and rape made me feel detached from the book and the so-called love story in it.<br><br>All in all, it seems that I am not a good reader of dark books &amp; mafia stories and I will stay away from those in the future and I will not try any more books from this writer again. This was my first and last.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1524009437ra/25393874.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></span>
  <a data-text-id="14190295981192304821" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_3584864016" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/3584864016" />
    <a title="K" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/87787809-k"><img alt="K" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1606080943p2/87787809.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/3584864016?book_show_action=true">Oct 11, 2020</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="K" class="user" itemprop="url" name="K" href="/user/show/87787809-k">K</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Paperback 1506110916" href="/book/show/24449343-raze">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/87787809-k?shelf=mafia-romance">mafia-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/87787809-k?shelf=fast-paced">fast-paced</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/87787809-k?shelf=hurt-my-heart-crushed-my-soul">hurt-my-heart-crushed-my-soul</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer3584864016" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10572345481322489878">5 <b>“Lyubov moya” + “Solnyshko”</b> STARS!!!!!<br/><br/>Bittersweet but beautiful, so brutally beautiful. That’s pretty much all things RAZE for me, and exactly what I felt it was while reading and experiencing my first ever Tillie Cole novel.<br/><br/><b>‘Mama always said the stars aligned when we were born, that God made us a match. From the first time we saw each other, Luka took me in his arms and swore his protection over me to my mother. Mama used to say she caught him staring into my crib only hours after I was born.</b></span>
  <span id="freeText10572345481322489878" style="display:none">5 <b>“Lyubov moya” + “Solnyshko”</b> STARS!!!!!<br /><br />Bittersweet but beautiful, so brutally beautiful. That’s pretty much all things RAZE for me, and exactly what I felt it was while reading and experiencing my first ever Tillie Cole novel.<br /><br /><b>‘Mama always said the stars aligned when we were born, that God made us a match. From the first time we saw each other, Luka took me in his arms and swore his protection over me to my mother. Mama used to say she caught him staring into my crib only hours after I was born. Then when she asked him what he was doing, he asked her if he could have me. My mama joked and told him it would be my choice when I was old enough to crawl, and from the minute I was old enough to crawl, my mama told me I only ever crawled to one boy…Luka Tolstoi.’</b><br /><br />Soulmates.<br />Star-crossed lovers.<br /><b>Luka Jakob Tolstoi</b> and <b>Kisa-Anna Volkova</b>.<br />These two were always meant to be together, have always belonged to one another. Just irrevocably each other’s, the intrinsically other half to both their hearts, bodies, and souls. From mere, very young children of only a couple years to early teenagers living and breathing their first love, even in the midst of a bloodthirsty Bratva life, Kisa and Luka’s manifest connection was always something otherworldly.<br /><br /><b>‘Luka’s beautiful gaze met mine and his lips parted with a brief exhale. “Because you belong to me, Kisa. You always have.” Luka’s face thawed and he pointed at my eye, then his left. “You’re a part of me, remember? God put a piece of you within me so when we were born, everyone would know we matched.”</b><br /><br />Years pass, in which, the two childhood sweethearts have long been violently torn away from each other. Ripped apart at the seams and left with respective traumas and nothing but numbness. Until, one fateful night, they meet again. Only, this time around, everything is like nothing before. And things have changed for the worse. So gut-wrenchingly worse. But soulmates are soulmates and as long as Kisa and Luka’s remember each other’s, all cannot be lost no matter how hopeless and damned everything surrounding appears to be.<br /><br /><b>‘It was dangerous. It was haunting. It was forbidden. And although it was wrong, it felt perfectly right.’</b><br /><br />While being quite predictable, RAZE turned out to be so much more, namely in the way it made me feel. So deeply, so intensely. For some time, everything about it felt perpetually bittersweet, because for every sweet and heartfelt moment, the brutal reality of its dark nature would follow, punishingly and mercilessly. It is, after all, a tragically romantic and heartbreakingly dark tale of love. But for all its heartache and devastation, it does give Kisa and Luka their happy ending and thank God because it is so needed. Beyond lovely and just everything for the two once broken souls who find, in each other, all that they need to heal and feel truly alive again. All in all, Raze broke my heart but healed it, and I’m wholeheartedly pleased with my first—by-this-author—read.<br /><br /><b>‘She was a balm, my calm. My Kisa-Anna.’</b></span>
  <a data-text-id="10572345481322489878" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_1062107778" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1062107778" />
    <a title="~♡AB♡~" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/12180287-ab"><img alt="~♡AB♡~" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1555104554p2/12180287.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1062107778?book_show_action=true">Sep 23, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="~♡AB♡~" class="user" itemprop="url" name="~♡AB♡~" href="/user/show/12180287-ab">~♡AB♡~</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12180287-ab?shelf=dark-erotica">dark-erotica</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12180287-ab?shelf=4-star-reads-really-really-good">4-star-reads-really-really-good</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12180287-ab?shelf=fighters">fighters</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12180287-ab?shelf=friend-s-brother-or-brothers-friend">friend-s-brother-or-brothers-friend</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12180287-ab?shelf=mafia-mofos">mafia-mofos</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1062107778" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3040456144032076294">★★★★ <b>4 Stars</b> ★★★★ <br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1420064449i/13163092._SY540_.jpg' width='400' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>Intense</b> is the first word that springs to mind when describing this book and I have a thing for big brooding men who exude dangerous so it was definitely something that I knew I was going to love, plus it's written by Tillie Cole who just happens to be on my list of authors that I will automatically read.<br/><br/><b>Raze</b> has been imprisoned since he was a boy, a <b>death match fighter</b> who is under the rule of the Georgians. His memory blocked and his emotions erased, he is a fighting machine </span>
  <span id="freeText3040456144032076294" style="display:none">★★★★ <b>4 Stars</b> ★★★★ <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1420064449i/13163092._SY540_.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Intense</b> is the first word that springs to mind when describing this book and I have a thing for big brooding men who exude dangerous so it was definitely something that I knew I was going to love, plus it's written by Tillie Cole who just happens to be on my list of authors that I will automatically read.<br><br><b>Raze</b> has been imprisoned since he was a boy, a <b>death match fighter</b> who is under the rule of the Georgians. His memory blocked and his emotions erased, he is a fighting machine that only knows how to survive in hell on earth.<br><br><b>Kisa</b>, the daughter of one of the three "Red" Bratva Kings of New York is in a forced relationship with an abusive man, also imprisoned by fate and family duty.<br><br>When Raze flees his hell-hole, he has only one thing on his mind - <b>REVENGE</b>, but revenge leads him to something else when he saves Kisa from an attack something in him rises to the surface and that is a protectiveness that is so <i>fierce</i> that he doesn't know how to deal with it.<br><br>I loved how Kisa taught Raze how to feel again, it was so beautiful to watch this big strong man turn from an anger filled bitter hulk to someone so tender and loving. <br><br><blockquote>
  <b>"I'm closing my eyes so I can feel being inside you." He placed his hand over his heart and rasped out, "I've seen too many bad things with these eyes. This, I will feel in my heart."</b>
</blockquote><br><br>Overall, it was a great stand-alone dark romance that will leave you breathless and despite it's predictability and the slight repetitiveness it was the perfect read for me.</span>
  <a data-text-id="3040456144032076294" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

//<![CDATA[  

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('JWdkEgaz3oA/sk64g/XQgT+JPlvyB+UaLVo/Xv6ZSOlhmRoArkqjtrq4/2cPSHbloQkiaJ5YrhVZKxWG/66LGw==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('Swqg892N/WC5tDpyiMQ5FNLlHu87A/rnvWUUIu1u5C4P9N7hdXSAVjy+i60EeZ9wTGUC3FdcsejJFD767Fkn3A==')})
  }
//]]>
</script>

      <div id="aboutAuthor" class=" clearFloats bigBox"><div class="h2Container gradientHeaderContainer"><h2 class="brownBackground"><a href="/author/show/7074846.Tillie_Cole">About Tillie Cole</a></h2></div><div class="bigBoxBody"><div class="bigBoxContent containerWithHeaderContent">
          <div class='bookAuthorProfile'>
<div class='bookAuthorProfile__topContainer'>
<div class='bookAuthorProfile__photoContainer'>
<a href="/author/show/7074846.Tillie_Cole"><div class='bookAuthorProfile__photo' style='background-image: url(https://images.gr-assets.com/authors/1517004382p3/7074846.jpg);'></div>
</a></div>
<div class='bookAuthorProfile__widgetContainer'>
<div class='bookAuthorProfile__name'>
<a href="/author/show/7074846.Tillie_Cole">Tillie Cole
</a></div>
<div class='goodreadsAuthorBadge'></div>
<div class='bookAuthorProfile__followerCount'>
13,960
followers
</div>

</div>
</div>
<div class='bookAuthorProfile__about'>

<span id="freeTextContainer11631891768323478542">Amazon & USA Today Best Selling Author, Tillie Cole, is a Northern girl through and through. She originates from a place called Teesside on that little but awesomely sunny (okay I exaggerate) Isle called Great Britain. She was brought up surrounded by her English rose mother -- a farmer's daughter, her crazy Scottish father, a savagely sarcastic sister and a multitude of rescue animals and horses.</span>
  <span id="freeText11631891768323478542" style="display:none">Amazon &amp; USA Today Best Selling Author, Tillie Cole, is a Northern girl through and through. She originates from a place called Teesside on that little but awesomely sunny (okay I exaggerate) Isle called Great Britain. She was brought up surrounded by her English rose mother -- a farmer's daughter, her crazy Scottish father, a savagely sarcastic sister and a multitude of rescue animals and horses. <br />Being a scary blend of Scottish and English, Tillie embraces both cultures; her English heritage through her love of HP sauce and freshly made Yorkshire Puddings, and her Scottish which is mostly demonstrated by her frighteningly foul-mouthed episodes of pure rage and her much loved dirty jokes.<br /><br />Having been born and raised as a Teesside Smoggie, Tillie, at age nineteen, moved forty miles north to the 'Toon', Newcastle-Upon-Tyne, where she attended Newcastle University and graduated with a Bachelor of Arts honours degree in Religious Studies. She returned two years later to complete a Post-Graduate Certificate in Teaching High School Social Studies. Tillie, regards Newcastle to be a home from home and enjoyed the Newcastle Geordie way of life for seven 'proper mint' and 'lush' years.<br /><br />One summers day, after finishing reading her thousandth book on her much loved and treasured Kindle, Tillie turned to her husband and declared, "D'you know, I have a great idea for a story. I could write a book." Several months later, after repeating the same tired line at the close of another completed story, she was scolded by her husband to shut up talking about writing a novel and "just bloody do it!" For the first time in eleven years, Tillie actually took his advice (he is still trying to get over the shock) and immediately set off on a crazy journey, delving deep into her fertile imagination. <br /><br />Tillie, ever since, has written from the heart. She combines her passion for anything camp and glittery with her love of humour and dark brooding men (most often muscled and tattooed – they’re her weakness!). She also has a serious side (believe it or not!) and loves to immerse herself in the complex study of World Religions, History and Cultural Studies and creates fantasy stories that enable her to thread serious issues and topics into her writing -- yep, there's more to this girl than profanity and sparkles!<br /><br />After six years of teaching high school Social Studies and following her Professional Rugby Player husband around Europe, they have finally given up their nomadic way of life and settled in Calgary, Alberta where Tillie spends most of her days (and many a late night) lost in a writing euphoria or pursuing a dazzling career as a barrel-racing, tasselled-chap wearing, Stetson-sporting cowgirl... Ye-haw!<br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="11631891768323478542" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

</div>
</div>
